Important Foreign Telegrams Two

Greek Alliance Land Policy Success

Eastern European Situation Changes

National News, Ankara, October 28th. Greek Prime Minister Venizelos's visit to Turkey to discuss and establish a treaty of friendship is considered a great success. After Mr. Venizelos met with the Turkish President and Foreign Minister, the Turkish Prime Minister held a grand banquet today to formally welcome them. Speeches from both sides emphasized the importance of friendship between the two countries and the satisfying results of the continuous meetings. Turkish newspapers also expressed a warm welcome, saying that this move is not only important in the Near East, but also in the entire Europe and the world. Mr. Venizelos is a major European statesman who has always strongly opposed Turkey. His personal arrival in the Turkish capital carrying the banner of peace is sufficient to show that Greece's foreign policy has fundamentally changed, and Turkey's political position in Europe and internationally is becoming increasingly important.

Mussolini's Speech Like Throwing a Bomb

Hopes for International Disarmament Turned to Ashes

German Newspaper Views Pro and Con

Stock Market Situation Initially Affected

Commemoration Day of the Fascist March on Rome

All of Italy Celebrates Madly

National News Agency, Berlin, October 28th. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's speech on Monday commemorating the Fascist March on Rome was like throwing a large bomb into the European political arena, turning the world's various hopes for the International League of Nations Disarmament Preparatory Committee into ashes. This preparatory committee is the final committee meeting before convening the Disarmament Conference. Therefore, so far only Italian newspapers have warmly welcomed Mussolini's speech and his order to advance and spread Fascism throughout Europe, viewing it as Mussolini's strong determination to lead Italy to permanently reside among the world's first-class countries. This is in contrast to the lip service of politicians from other countries, who constantly speak of peace, cooperation, and alliance, but actually condone cabinet members in using what they call huge sums of money necessary to repair wartime losses to expand armaments and threaten neighboring countries. As for German newspapers, their views are mixed. The right-wing newspapers, especially the National Socialist newspapers, praised his proposal to revise the treaty, which shows friendship towards Germany. The right-wing and liberal newspapers were mostly cold and sarcastic, asking how the Southern Tyrol region of Italy, which was seized from Austria, will be handled, and refuting the idea that the world and Germany can be saved by Fascism or other forms of dictatorship. The German Newspaper, the organ of the Central Clerical Party, often representing the views of Catholic leaders, also condemned Mussolini's ambition to spread Fascism throughout Europe, saying that some of his words must be regarded as interference in Germany's internal affairs and are not friendly acts towards a friendly country. Furthermore, the semi-official Foreign Political Communication News stated that this speech was more moderate and valuable than Mussolini's previous speeches, and it was sufficient to express Italy's attitude on several diplomatic and political issues related to Germany. However, the newspaper also disagreed with his words regarding the Fascist movement.

National News Agency, Berlin, October 28th. Today, the stock market situation on the stock exchange fluctuated, because Mussolini's speech caused concerns about the current European political situation and the world economic life.

National News Agency, Rome, October 28th. Today is the anniversary of the Fascist March on Rome. All of Italy is celebrating enthusiastically. This year, three thousand public buildings are having completion or naming ceremonies. The new station in Genoa, built with 17 million lire, is also among them. This afternoon, Mussolini personally inspected the parade of the Blackshirts. In the evening, the streets of the capital are brightly lit with electric lights, and there are crowds of tourists. The area near Mussolini's private residence is particularly crowded.

Continuing Reports on the Aboriginal Resistance in Taiwan

Occupation of Mt. Nōkō's Watershed

Local Authorities Busy Dispatching Troops and Police

Dentsu, Taipei, 28th—Regarding the Wushe aboriginal rebellion, according to later reports, on the morning of the 27th at 8:00 AM, a group of several hundred aborigines led by a chieftain named Mōraru attacked the athletic meet at the Wushe Public School, brutally murdering some twenty-odd people including Nōkō District Magistrate Ogasawara, school staff, and police officers who were in attendance. Subsequently, they indiscriminately massacred local mainland Chinese and Taiwanese, and attacked the police precinct, seizing 170 rifles and 300 rounds of ammunition. They then prepared for battle, planning to attack Pulishe. Upon receiving the report, the Taichung police requested reinforcements from the Taipei, South, and North police. The Onizumi Company stationed in Taichung also urgently departed for Puli. In addition, Hualien Port dispatched 80 infantrymen and 50 police officers to attack the aboriginal villages from three sides. Operations commenced on the morning of the 29th. About 270 mainland Chinese and 430 Taiwanese reside in the area at the center of the disturbances. As of last night, only 140 have escaped. The safety of the rest is unknown. The Susha aborigines, who belong to the Atayal people, number 2,170 in total, all from local villages. Many other aborigines reside near these villages. This rebellion is an isolated action by the Wushe aborigines and is not related to others. Puli has already begun defensive measures. Iron netting has been laid between Puli and Wushe, and electrified. Police, local militia, Taiwanese, and various organizations are cooperating in the guard.

Japan Associated Press, Tokyo, 29th—The Colonial Ministry received a telegram stating that at 8:00 AM on the 29th, police units had expelled the aborigines and occupied Wushe. According to an official gazette from the Taiwan Governor-General's Office on the same day, the aborigines have attacked the outposts on the western side of Mt. Nōkō from today and occupied Mt. Nōkō's watershed. 150 police officers in the vicinity have advanced to East Nōkō. According to an announcement by the Taiwan Governor-General's Police Bureau, the cause of this disturbance seems to be the recent frequent incidents of forced labor. Others say that a Class B police officer from a certain village started the uprising due to resentment over unequal monthly wages. An investigation is currently underway. The Colonial Ministry received a telegram stating that of the 17 Wushe outposts, as many as 13 have been attacked by aborigines.

Dentsu, Taipei, 29th—According to a report obtained by the Taiwan Army Command, the Takai Unit and the Kudo Unit, which were dispatched to suppress the Wushe aborigines, occupied the aboriginal front line village of Riqing around 1:00 AM today. They then cooperated with army aircraft in a fierce battle, occupying Wushe at 8:05 AM. The aborigines fled into the nearby mountains, continuing to resist from the high ground. Another telegram stated that the Takai Unit, which occupied Wushe this morning, immediately began recovering the bodies of the murdered Japanese. The body of District Magistrate Ogasawara, who was in Wushe at the time, was found murdered on a bridge north of Wushe, hidden under the bridge. By noon, a total of 183 bodies had been found, including 38 children. The manner of death was extremely gruesome. Survivors are hiding in the bushes, etc. The aborigines indiscriminately slaughtered both Japanese and Taiwanese, carrying food and supplies into the deep mountains. After the mountain artillery arrives, they will launch a fierce attack on the hiding areas.

Reuters, Tokyo, 29th—According to news from Taiwan, about 140 Japanese police and civilians have died in the uprising of the Taiwanese aborigines. However, this has not been confirmed due to telephone interruptions. The aborigines previously revolted in 1920 and have since lived peacefully. The cause of this uprising is unknown. Some say it is due to overly strict police control. Others say that a certain company recently agreed to borrow 45 million Japanese yen from the American Morgan Company and plans to build a large dam somewhere to build a hydroelectric power plant. If this plan is implemented, it will flood several square miles of aboriginal residential areas, forcing the aborigines to relocate, so they gathered to resist. According to an official telegram from Taiwan, of the more than 200 Japanese residing in the affected area, only 16 escaped. Of the 400 Taiwanese, only 112 escaped. It is feared that the rest have been killed.

Nehru Sentenced to Imprisonment and Fine

Reuters, Allahabad, 29th—All-India Congress Committee President Nehru, not long after being released from prison, was arrested by police at a meeting here on October 19 while giving a speech. Today, the court sentenced him to two years of imprisonment with hard labor and a large fine for inciting the public and urging people to break the salt laws and refuse to pay taxes.

Reuters, Delhi, 29th—This morning, police arrested three men and one woman, seizing four bomb casings, one handgun, many bullets, chemicals, and seditious documents.

German Federal Council Foreign Affairs Committee Meets

Communist Party Member Proposes a Motion to Stop Paying Reparations

Government Representatives Account for Only a Small Minority, Situation Unfavorable

National News Agency, Berlin, 29th—The German Federal Council's Foreign Affairs Committee began its meeting today. The position of the government representatives is extremely precarious. Even with the support of the Social Democrats, they remain in the minority. The representatives attending on behalf of the government are Foreign Minister Curtius, along with the Finance and Justice Ministers. The most noteworthy item on the agenda is the Communist Party's proposal to immediately halt the payment of reparations stipulated in the Young Plan. It is expected that this proposal will receive unanimous support from the Nationalist Party and the National Socialist Party. If so, it is bound to pass with a majority vote. However, even if it passes in the committee, it is unlikely to be implemented, as the case still needs to be considered by the full council. It seems that there is no doubt that this case will be rejected by the full council.

Brazilian Military Government's Proclamation to the People

Dissolving Congress is Inevitable

International Treaties Will Certainly Be Respected

Pacific Press, Rio de Janeiro, 28th—The military group issued a proclamation to the Brazilian people, stating that the dissolution of Congress and the granting of amnesty are the results of the successful revolution. Once President Vargas arrives in the capital, they will be announced and implemented. Furthermore, the orders to cease hostilities and restore peace have already been issued. It also stated that order and tranquility must be maintained, justice must be upheld, treaties must be respected, and unity must be maintained.

Reuters, Rio de Janeiro, 29th—It is learned that in this Brazilian revolution, a total of 1,000 people died in the battles from October 15 to 20.

Heavy Rain, Snow, and Hail in Lower Silesia

Rivers Overflow, Drowning People and Livestock

National News Agency, Berlin, 28th—In Lower Silesia, Germany, incessant heavy rain mixed with snow and hail has caused rivers to overflow. Many bridges and embankments have been destroyed. The lower reaches of the Oder River have become a flooded area, with no fewer than several thousand houses submerged. Many people and livestock have drowned. However, due to telephone disruptions, there are no detailed reports.

Berlin Metalworkers Resume Work

Reuters, Berlin, 28th—The 275 metalworking factories in Berlin, employing a total of 120,000 workers, who went on strike on October 15, have resumed work today because both sides have agreed to submit the dispute to arbitration. It is learned that the workers lost a total of 10 million marks in wages during this strike.

Japanese Ministry of Finance's Demand for Savings

Army and Navy Departments Collude to Resist

Dentsu, Tokyo, 29th—The Ministry of Finance's review proposal requires the Army and Navy to save a total of 86 million yen. The Army is indignant at its unreasonableness, especially the hardliners in the General Staff, who claim that this is a despotic act of the Ministry of Finance giving undue weight to economic matters, and disregarding the Empire's national defense policy. They advocate that the Army and Navy should cooperate in the future and negotiate with the Ministry of Finance with a resolute attitude. If the relationship between the government and the military becomes complicated, the government and the party will do their best to attack or publicize the military's tyranny. Therefore, the Army and Navy should also share joint responsibility, clarify the military's position, and await fair criticism. The General Staff believes that it is the duty of those who are directly responsible for national defense and advocate that the Army and Navy jointly resist.

Bulgarian King Returns Home by Ship with Queen

Encountering a Strong Gale, Communication Severed

National News Agency, Sofia, 28th—The Bulgarian King, after going to Italy to marry, has returned home by ship with the new Queen on the Ferdinando di Savoia. However, no wireless reports from the ship have been received here, and the public is quite anxious. However, no other ships have been heard to have received distress signals from the ship, and it is believed that they are safe en route. It is likely that the wireless communication was interrupted due to the strong winds. The people here have prepared a grand welcoming ceremony, and are somewhat disappointed by the long wait for news of the King and Queen. Especially as it is late autumn, florists are finding it difficult to find another batch of fresh flowers at this time.

National News

Navy Ministry Convenes Fleet Maneuvers

In recent years, the Navy Ministry has attached great importance to the training of officers and soldiers. Last autumn, on the anniversary of the first uprising of the Prime Minister, Acting Minister of the Navy Chen Shaokuan personally led various ships to Zhejiang waters for maneuvers, with excellent results. Recently, Chen Shaokuan also plans to concentrate various ships and boats and head to the Zhejiang waters for large-scale maneuvers. The ministry has now telegraphed the following ships that have arrived in Beijing one after another: Chuyou, Jiangzhen, Chuqian, Jiangyuan, Chuguan, and Chutai, as well as the Chenzi, Hu'e, Suzi, Yongsheng, Hudiao, and Huying boats, and the Ding'an transport ship. All are concentrated in the Baguazhou area and began maneuvers on the 23rd, with Chen personally directing from the Chuyou flagship, and instructing all ships and boats to follow the methods of front-line combat during the maneuvers, and officers and soldiers are not allowed to leave the ship. At dawn on the 23rd, Acting Minister Chen ordered the soldiers of each ship and boat to practice sampans, at 10:00 AM, to practice fire fighting off the ship, and in the afternoon, all the team's more than 20 sampans practiced sailing. On the morning of the 24th, Chen summoned the deputy captains of each ship and boat to the Chuyou flagship for instructions, and taught them the essentials of managing sampans, as well as the summary of flag and light signals, and encouraged the deputy captains to actively promote soldiers' physical education and public health. Afterwards, he continued to operate the sampans and ordered the rifle teams of each ship to land and practice military exercises, and the sampans to practice anchor drifting. In the afternoon, the whole team practiced collision and leak plugging, as well as the army's communication flag signals. In the evening, they practiced the army's communication light signals. At midnight, Chen personally went to the Chuqian warship and sounded the alarm, summoning officers and soldiers to practice fire drills. The soldiers of the ship were able to be ready in a hurry, and Chen praised them deeply. Later, he returned to the Chuyou flagship and suddenly ordered the soldiers of each ship and boat to carry out a large-scale attack and defense, and to perform searchlights. On the morning of the 25th, the whole team continued to practice fire fighting. In the afternoon, the soldiers of each ship held various sports activities, and in the evening, they practiced the army's communication light signals. On the morning of the 26th, Sunday, Acting Minister Chen inspected the trainees of each ship and boat, and encouraged each student to work hard in training, in order to deepen their knowledge and not fail the country's cultivation and the painstaking efforts of their superiors. At midnight, when the sky was full of stars, Chen summoned all the trainees to observe the planets and explained the relationship between navigation and astronomy. On the morning of the 27th, an enlarged Prime Minister's Memorial Week was convened at the Torpedo Camp, with 700 to 800 officers and soldiers from each ship and boat in attendance. Chen presided over the meeting, performed the ceremony as usual, and then gave instructions. Immediately after returning to the ship, he ordered the soldiers to practice sailing the sampans, raising and lowering the sails, and floating in the river. The soldiers had been through the wind and waves for a long time, and their spirits were doubled. Then they practiced the international communication flag signals. In the afternoon, Chen led the sampans of each ship to practice various ship formations, such as single file and echelon formation. The formations changed quickly and the orders were carried out. The captains of each ship and boat directed well, and the soldiers were well trained. In the evening, they practiced international communication light signals, as well as fire extinguishing night battles, defense against ship sieges, and searchlights. On the morning of the 28th, the soldiers of each ship and boat landed for maneuvers. In the afternoon, Chen summoned the deputy captains for instructions and gave instructions on the key points of sampan storage and equipment, and then held a sampan military exercise. During the exercise, the sound of gunfire was loud, as if facing a great enemy. In the evening, they practiced water targets, and the results were excellent. At dawn on the 29th, the whole army held soft exercises. At 10:00 AM, the sampans practiced anchor drifting. In the afternoon, it stopped due to rain. In addition to participating in various exercises, each ship and boat also practiced torpedo shooting, practicing from morning to night without stopping. Their spirit and military discipline were excellent. It is said that this exercise will last for another week. Chen Shaokuan plans to personally lead the entire fleet to Zhejiang waters for formal maneuvers. It is expected that the results will be even more impressive.

Chronicle of the Great Battle Near Nanning

Guangdong Army Prepares to Attack Liuzhou, Guangxi Army Changes Defense Lines

Guangzhou correspondence, the war in Nanning has recently become more intense. Zhang Guijiun believes that since Yan and Feng in the north have fallen, he is afraid of being isolated in Guangxi, so he is desperately fighting for Nanning in order to make a final struggle. At the beginning of this month, he began to use plainclothes teams to attack the 10th and 8th Route Armies surrounding Nanning. The fighting between the two sides was intermittent. Unexpectedly, on the 16th, Zhang Guijiun's army in Liuzhou launched another large-scale attack. The destinations were Nanning and Guixian. From the morning of the 16th, the Wei Yunsong and Huang Xuchu troops in Nanning City first rushed out of the city and attacked the 10th Route Guangxi Army four times in succession. At about 10:00 AM on the same day, more than 10,000 Guangxi troops from Qianjiang, Laibin, and other places in Liuzhou, including Liang Chaoji and Mo Shujie's troops and Zhang Jun and Xue Yue's troops, rushed straight to the city. From then on, they attacked the Guangxi Army from inside and outside. The Guangxi Army's Lu Han, Zhu Xu, and Zhang Chong divisions fought separately. Although the positions were all occupied by Zhang Guijiun's army, they still fought fiercely for three days and nights. By dawn on the 19th, the Guangxi Army's baggage and supplies had suffered heavy losses, and they changed their strategy, temporarily shortening the defense line. Liang Chaoji, Xue Yue, and other troops immediately entered Nanning and joined forces with the Huang and Wei troops in the city. At present, one part of the Guangxi Army has retreated to the fortress more than 20 miles outside Yongcheng, and another part has retreated to the Shibu Genzhuzhou Taiping area to concentrate, and will join forces with the 8th Route Army to attack after replenishment. During the great battle near Nanning, at the same time, the Guangxi Army's Yang Tenghui troops attacked the 8th Route Army's Yu Hanmou troops in Binyang's rear. Xu Shi immediately sent Li Zhenqiu's brigade to Silong to fight. Also, the Guangxi Army's Liang Hansong troops led four regiments to disturb the Dacun Market in Guixian on the 19th (about 20 miles from Litang). The 8th Route Army's Chen Hanguang regiment stationed in Litang went to resist. The two sides fought fiercely until the evening of the 22nd, with more than 1,000 casualties, and were defeated by Chen's regiment. The Guangxi Army's Liang troops retreated to above the Dacun Market. In Silong, the two sides also fought fiercely for three days. The Guangxi Army's Yang troops suffered more losses. At present, they have failed and returned to Shanglin. According to news from the front, the front-line war is still very tense. Chen Jitang, the commander-in-chief of the 8th Route Army, personally went to Taozhou on the 21st to plan the offensive strategy, and convened a military meeting with front-line generals Huang Renhuan, Yu Hanmou, Chen Hanguang, Li Yangjing, and Fan Dexing. He returned to Wu on the same day and telegraphed the commander of the 4th Fleet, Chen Ce, to go to Wu to discuss sending the fleet to the front to help in the war. Chen Riji will lead the fleet west. On the land front, due to the outbreak of the war, the vanguard Yu and Huang troops will advance to Xiangxian and Liuqing. The rear troops of the 8th Route Army should advance to fill the defense. The 63rd Division's Huang Zhiwen brigade stationed in Pingnan was transferred to Guixian to join the front line. The Lin Bin troops of the replenishment regiment stationed in Wu were sent to Guiping to help defend. Also, two regiments of the Independent Brigade Zhang Ruigui troops transferred from the rear will depart from Zhaoqing for Wuzhou on a specific day to take over the Lin regiment's defense areas of Huoshan Fuhekou and Tengjiangkou. At present, there are Peng Guangting's Special Service Battalion stationed at the airport in Wuzhou, the 2nd Battalion of the 1st Regiment of the 1st Independent Brigade stationed in Hexianzhou, the artillery company of the regiment stationed in Sanjiaozui, the machine gun company stationed at the former British Consulate, and the 1st and 2nd Battalions of the 63rd Division's Education Regiment stationed in Duhe Huoshan. The various companies of the 3rd Battalion of the Independent Brigade are stationed in the Shizi Fort, Lengshuidong, and Dalikou, and the defense is very tight. (October 24)

Atrocities of Japanese Students in Qingdao

Beating and Injuring Tiezong Students and Injuring Police

Surrounding the Police Station and Destroying the Office

Qingdao correspondence, on the 24th of this month, Tiezong students and Japanese middle school students held an autumn international sports basketball preliminary competition at the Huiquan Sports Field. As a result, Tiezong won by a large margin of 32 to 12. After the Japanese middle school failed, they became angry and provoked trouble for no reason. While on the court, they kicked and injured Tiezong student Yu Zhixin's legs in several places, and stepped on and injured Jiang Xiling's feet in two places. After the end, they searched everywhere for Tiezong students with the intention of fighting. In the end, with the maintenance of the referees of the international sports meeting, no accident occurred. Unexpectedly, at about 6:00 PM on the same afternoon, Tiezong students Liu Zhende and Yu Yikui were walking home from school when they came to the middle section of Jiangsu Road. Suddenly, more than a dozen Japanese middle school students surrounded Liu and Yu, punching and kicking them, kicking Liu Zhende in the face and knocking out several teeth, causing blood to flow like a fountain. Fortunately, two students from Lixian Middle School rushed to mediate and found police officer Xing Jiying of the 15th Police Station of the Public Security Bureau who tried his best to dissuade them. At this time, more and more Japanese students gathered, about 40 in total, relying on their strength to commit violence and disobeying persuasion. They even pressed police officer Xing Jiying to the ground and beat him severely, tearing off his collar badge and tearing a piece of his uniform. Seeing that he could not stop them, the police officer broke through the encirclement and returned to the station to report. Students Liu Zhen, Yu Yikui, outnumbered, also fled to the station to temporarily avoid the fierce attack. Unexpectedly, the Japanese students saw Tiezong students fleeing into the station and immediately surrounded the station. A Japanese middle school teacher was directing from the side. Seeing the menacing situation, the patrol chief of the station immediately reported to the First Branch Bureau and telegraphed Tiezong and the Japanese Consulate. At this time, Japanese student Takahashi Kenichi led more than a dozen people including Takeda Yoshijutsu, Hayashida Takeshi, and Hayashida Kiyoshi, and forcibly broke into the office, overturning all the indoor equipment and making a mess. Fortunately, Sun Bingxian, the director of the First Branch Bureau, and patrol officer Shi Zhengfa of the relevant branch station rushed to the scene with police, and the Japanese Consulate also sent a staff member, Hirayama Isamu, with two Japanese police officers to the scene to help. They first persuaded more than a hundred Chinese and Japanese students to disperse, and finally prevented a major disaster from occurring. Director Sun also took Japanese student Takahashi Kenichi and Tiezong student Liu Zhende to the bureau for detailed questioning. In addition to sending the injured students and police to the Pujji Hospital for treatment, the Public Security Bureau has submitted a request to the municipal government to negotiate with the Japanese Consul. It is heard that Tiezong has also reported the above situation in detail to the Jiaoji Railway Education Committee to make a serious protest to the Japanese side. (October 27)

Rampage of Communist Bandits He Long and Kuang Jixun

He Jian Urgently Transfers Various Armies to Encircle and Suppress

Changsha correspondence, the communist chieftains He Long and Kuang Jixun and their tens of thousands of followers are causing havoc in the Nanhua Bay An of Hunan Province and the Gongshi Jianli area of Hubei Province. Although the troops of Hunan and Hubei provinces have repeatedly suppressed them, they are always striking here and fleeing there, and their power is growing daily. They once captured Nanhua and occupied Gongshi twice. The people on the borders of the two provinces are suffering greatly. Recently, Hubei Province dispatched Lai Xinhui, Li Yunlong, and others to Gongshi Jianli to carry out a large-scale suppression. However, the Nanhua area of Hunan Province is guarded by local militias and no large army is stationed there. He and Kuang took advantage of the emptiness on the 21st and entered Hunan from Shishou County, attacking Nanhua in two routes. Kuang's bandits attacked Nanxian from Yu. He's bandits attacked Huarong from Xiankou. The local defense force was weak and could not resist. Nanhua and Nanxian were captured simultaneously at noon on the 22nd. The county magistrates and local defense forces of the two counties retreated to the Babai Gong area and telegraphed the province for help. Nanhua was originally the richest area in the lake area and the central hub of the lake area. With Nanhua captured, Changde, Hanshou, Yuanjiang, and Anxiang were shaken, and they also telegraphed the province to request troops to suppress them. He Jian arrived in the province by plane from Hankou at 10:00 AM on the 24th. After receiving the urgent report, he immediately transferred troops to block and suppress them in separate routes: (1) Telegraph to Director He of Hankou to send a large army to block and intercept in the Shishou and Gong'an areas on the border of Hubei, and order the Lai Xinhui's Zhang Ying division, which is currently arriving in Anxiang, Hunan, to attack Nanxian; (2) Telegraph to Chen Quzhen, the first garrison commander, to send two regiments of troops to attack Huarong along the lake from Jinshi; (3) Telegraph to Dai Huiyuan, the commander of the suppression of bandits in western Hunan, to transfer troops to attack Nanhua from Changde; (4) Telegraph to the county magistrates of Yuanjiang and Hanshou to quickly gather local militias to flank and attack Nanhua. The above-mentioned troops will arrive by about the 26th, and it is expected that the bandits will be repelled without difficulty.

Discovery of Bandits in Langxi County, Southern Anhui

Wuhu correspondence, the southeast village of Langxi County, southern Anhui, is adjacent to the border of Guangde County. A large number of communist bandits have recently been discovered, and they are very rampant. The towns of Biqiao, Taocheng, and Yaocun in the county have been robbed one after another. All the police and militia guns have been confiscated. They kill and set fires recklessly. In addition to the Langxi Chamber of Commerce telegraphing the central government and Chairman Chen Tiaoyuan, requesting that a large army be sent to suppress them quickly, they also telegraphed the Anhui Provincial Chamber of Commerce in this area for help. The Chamber of Commerce immediately telegraphed the provincial government and Yue Shi according to the situation, and sent troops overnight to suppress them in order to secure the local area. The original telegram reads: Anqing forwards to the Anhui Provincial Government Yue Shi's office, according to the Langxi County Chamber of Commerce telegram, "Our county's southeast border connects to Guangde, the communist bandits are rampant, the county seat is in danger, please urge the dispatch of a large army to suppress them, etc." According to this, it is appropriate to telegraph you for your review and approval, and quickly order the transfer of capable troops to go to defend and suppress them on a specific day to protect the local area. Anhui Provincial Chamber of Commerce Joint Kowtow Impression, (October 28)

Ministry of Finance Formulates Regulations for the Tobacco Unified Tax Bureau Organization

The Ministry of Finance promulgated the organization regulations for the Shandong Tobacco Unified Tax Bureau yesterday, which are recorded as follows: (Article 1) The Shandong Tobacco Unified Tax Bureau is directly under the Ministry and is headed by a Director and a Deputy Director, who shall, upon orders from the Ministry, handle the collection of the tobacco unified tax in all counties within Shandong. The staff of the Bureau shall be selected and appointed by the Director of the Bureau and reported to the Ministry for record. (Article 2) The tobacco unified tax is temporarily set at 3 yuan and 6 jiao per 100 jin, which shall be paid by the tobacco merchants in one lump sum, and a stamp and certificate shall be issued for circulation in various places without being re-collected. The above tax shall be borne by the tobacco merchants. All tobacco leaves produced by tobacco farmers shall be allowed to be freely sold to companies or tobacco vendors that buy tobacco. No collecting agency shall directly collect other taxes from farmers. If the buying location needs to be inspected by other bureaus, the Bureau may issue a temporary shipping order for verification. (Article 3) Rolling tobacco companies that buy tobacco or tobacco vendors that set up factories to buy tobacco shall report their names, factory locations, and the names of their managers to the Bureau for record. (Article 4) When buying tobacco, each tobacco company and each tobacco vendor shall report the quantity of goods purchased to the Bureau for registration, verify the number of jin per piece, pay the tax, and obtain a certificate, which shall be affixed to the tobacco package for inspection. (Article 5) When each tobacco company or each tobacco vendor ships tobacco, in addition to reporting to the Bureau, verifying the weight and quantity, paying the tax, and obtaining a certificate, the Bureau shall fill out a tax form and a duplicate receipt for collection before they are allowed to ship. (Article 6) The tobacco unified tax form and duplicate receipt shall be formulated by the Ministry, stamped with the Ministry's seal, and issued to the Bureau. The certificate and temporary shipping order shall be printed and issued by the Bureau for the time being. (Article 7) The Bureau may inspect the manufacture and sale of tobacco at any time to prevent fraud. (Article 8) Those who violate the provisions of these Articles and sell tobacco shall be subject to a fine, the rules for which shall be determined separately. (Article 9) If there are omissions in these Articles, the Ministry shall amend them at any time. Matters not stipulated shall be determined separately by detailed rules. (Article 10) These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Public Opening of the Siku Quanshu in Shenyang

Permission Granted for Citizens to Enter and Read

Shenyang Dispatch: The Siku Quanshu collection housed in the Wensu Pavilion within the Shenyang Imperial Palace is a rare treasure of Chinese culture. Previously, it had been placed under the management of the Dongbei (Northeast) Three Provinces Museum. Subsequently, due to the importance of the collection, the local authorities formed a Preservation Committee comprised of representatives from the Provincial Government, the Museum, the Library, and the Education Department. Liu Xinyi was appointed as the administrator. Recently, the Preservation Committee, in response to numerous requests for viewing from various quarters, decided that a public opening was necessary. Starting this week, citizens will be allowed to visit, provided they possess an official letter of introduction and adhere to the visiting rules. Over the past few days, visitors from all sectors have been arriving in a continuous stream, with those from the education and press circles being the most numerous. The visiting rules are as follows: (1) Visiting hours are from 10:00 AM to 3:00 PM every Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday. (2) Introductions for visitors are limited to official letters from military and political leaders of the province, or from formal public or private legal entities. (3) The visiting area is limited to the Wensu Pavilion's Siku Quanshu collection. (4) Visiting procedures: (a) Visitors must be escorted by the receptionist to the reception room; (b) Visitors must fill out the registration book prepared by the Pavilion; (c) Groups visiting must notify the Pavilion in advance for proper preparation, and if the number of people is too large, they must visit in groups to avoid overcrowding. (5) Visiting restrictions: (a) Smoking and carrying flammable items are prohibited; (b) Spitting and carrying dirty or unsanitary items are prohibited; (c) Taking photographs and carrying packages are prohibited.

Page 8

(d) Visitors are not allowed to enter areas without the guidance of the administrator; (e) Visitors are not allowed to browse through books that have not been opened by the administrator; (f) To ensure proper management, borrowing books from the Pavilion is strictly prohibited. (26th)

Reconstruction of the Northeast Airfield Implemented

Shenyang Dispatch: The Northeast Aviation Command's airfield, originally located near the Dongta Arsenal in Shenyang, has a total area of only about 700 meters east-west and only 500 meters north-south. Besides the hangars and factories, the remaining open space is too small and insufficient. Furthermore, the airfield is located near the arsenal's ammunition storage, and prolonged testing and engine noise can easily cause danger. In 1925, the former Aviation Office requested relocation to Beiling (North Tomb), but due to military exigencies and limited funds, it was not considered. This spring, the authorities resumed the previous proposal and actively proceeded with it, sending personnel to survey the wasteland of Beiling. It is estimated that the occupied civilian land includes areas of Sandaizi, Tianyitun, Guanyintun, Waziyao, Mamafen, and Baodaotun, totaling over 7,000 mu (approximately 1155 acres), of which over 1,000 mu are government land. The remaining civilian land has been evaluated by the Provincial Government upon consultation with the Chief Executive's Office, instructing Shenyang County to cooperate with the Aviation Command to assess the price for reporting, divided into three grades (120 yuan, 100 yuan, and 90 yuan per mu). Currently, the surveying and valuation matters have been completed and are awaiting pricing and purchasing. As for the surveyed site, it occupies 2,000 meters in each direction, calculated by surveying rope, about 900 bows on each side. Boundaries have been firmly established. It is planned to plant saplings around the perimeter to delineate the boundaries in the future. The construction of the airfield is said to commence in the spring of next year. All hangars, factories, and residential areas for office personnel will be built outside the airfield area. The Aviation Command dispatched Chief of Staff Yang Fengchun and the Shenyang County Public Security Bureau Chief Zhang Detang on the 22nd to conduct an inspection in order to plan everything. (October 24th)

Two Warships to Be Built for Northeast River Defense

Harbin Dispatch: It has been decided that the Northeast River Defense Fleet will have two warships built by the Northeast Shipbuilding Yard, with 300,000 silver dollars paid by the Northeast Navigation Bureau and the Northeast Navy River Transportation Office in three installments over three years. The shipyard has already received the blueprints and started work on the 16th of this month, first creating a model to be sent to the Navy Headquarters for review. The engines and boilers for both ships will be reused from old vessels. The displacement is set at 450 tons, the length is 180 feet, the height is 4 feet, the width is 30 feet, and the draft is 2 feet, making them larger and faster than the Lishui, Suisui, and Lijie ships. The armor plating will be 1.5 inches thick, the gun positions are set at four, and they will have a double-wheel stern. They will burn coal. The construction period is estimated at ten months, and it is expected to be completed around July of next year. As for the old warships Lijie and Jiangping, although they have been towed back to Harbin, they are irreparably damaged. Repairs are estimated to cost at least 300,000 yuan. Because the budget has not been finalized, they have not been repaired yet. The Jiangtai and Jiang'an ships have been towed to the dock for dismantling, and their parts will be used to supplement the new ships' needs. The Jiangheng and Lichuan are being salvaged in Fujin, but they have not yet been recovered due to the deep and fast-flowing waters there. The budget for the Northeast River Defense Fleet has changed several times, but the lack of funds in the Northeast has prevented ideal implementation. The Northeast Border Defense Command previously promised to allocate 1.5 million to add four ships, but due to the invasion of North China, which required huge amounts of money, the proposal was abandoned. Shen Honglie felt that the river defense fleet had only four incomplete ships, so he felt limited in strength both internally and externally. Thus, the Navigation Bureau and River Transportation Department devised a plan to add two ships. Considering the budget is only 300,000 yuan, one can know the capability of the new ships. (October 24th)

Local Dispatches

Songjiang

Oil Press Owner's Wife and Daughter Safe Return Home. Zhao Xichang's family, who used to run an oil press in Hujiaqiao, Punan, was previously kidnapped and suffered heavy losses, so the oil press had to close. On the 26th of last month, his sister Daguang was engaged and accompanied her mother, Madam Qin, to Songjiang to shop. The boat encountered pirates near Majing Port who pretended to inspect the cabin and abducted Madam Qin and her daughter along with their luggage and cash and fled. Her son, Xichang, being without money, did not seek assistance from various parties. He was rescued by the 4th Anti-Smuggling Squad Captain Pan Baozhong and Squad Leader Sheng, who sent Madam Qin and her daughter home by ship. However, the kidnappers have disappeared.

Dispute Over Additional 20% Housing Tax. The county Public Security Bureau's expenses are short by 131.5 yuan per month. The county previously ordered the First District Office to raise funds. The district replied that the housing tax revenue was insufficient. The county government then discussed methods of compensation at the last county administration meeting, resolving to order the First District Office to add 20% to the housing tax per household from October to compensate. The district's Housing and Police Tax Organization Committee discussed this at its ninth meeting. They believed that the Public Security Bureau was a county-wide matter and could not be borne by one district. Furthermore, the district's housing and police tax had recently been reorganized, and in May of this year, a special tax was levied for one month to repair the Public Security Bureau's buildings. At that time, merchants were repeatedly assured that there would be no further increases for the time being. Therefore, it was inconvenient to go back on their word. It was decided to have the district office reply to the county order to add 20%. It is expected that the county government will have to find other means of compensation.

Kidnapping Case in Jiashan Uncovered in Shanghai. According to a tip-off to the County Public Security Bureau about a kidnapping case, the detective Yang Shijie was secretly dispatched to Shanghai. Arriving at the address, he found a hostage named Wei Erguan, the 13-year-old son of Wei Zhangsheng of Weijialou, Li Ze Town, Jiashan, at the Chunjiang Inn behind the Great World in the French Concession. A kidnapper named Xie Aliuli was also captured in Taozhuang, Jiashan. He has been escorted back to the Public Security Bureau and will be transferred to the County Government's Anti-Banditry Bureau for interrogation.

Qixin's Bankruptcy Requires Investigation of Assets for Compensation. Qixin Sauce Garden in front of the Yue Temple went bankrupt last year due to losses. The creditors' lawsuit has not yet been resolved. The County Court has determined that there are many depositors and the bankruptcy involves a large amount of over 40,000 yuan. It has decided to send a letter to the Chamber of Commerce Chairman Cai Zhongyu, the Songjiang Bank Manager Xie Liangda, and the Shengyuan Trading Company Manager Tao Yisun to investigate the assets for proportionate compensation.

Wuxi

Investigate Road Damage on Yangyao Route. The section from Tingzi Bridge outside the East Gate to Yangyao outside the South Gate is an important thoroughfare for vehicles traveling north-south outside the city. Three years ago, when the privately established Wuxi Middle School first opened, it funded the road construction, allowing vehicles to pass without hindrance. However, recently, the side near the river has been privately damaged and used for planting vegetables by the Jiangbei Shantytown residents. The other side has been arbitrarily occupied and excavated for soil by nearby residents, resulting in a narrow road that is not only unable to allow vehicle crossings but is also very dangerous for pedestrians. Yesterday, the privately established Xizhong School sent a letter to the Municipal Engineering Office requesting a swift stop and restoration to the specified width according to the City Office's regulations. The City Engineering Office has approved the letter and forwarded it to the Public Security Bureau for strict enforcement and thorough investigation of the perpetrators.

Detention of Wounded Soldier Attempting to Rape Female Worker. There is a female worker named Liu Suzhen in a workshop outside the West Gate of Xiyi. She is young and beautiful. Unexpectedly, a wounded soldier saw her charm the other day and was immediately aroused. He broke into the workshop and threatened her in every way, intending to rape her. At that moment, Suzhen's brother, Liu Dexin, returned home from the outside and was greatly angered. He immediately stepped forward and twisted the wounded soldier into the jurisdiction of the 4th Public Security Bureau. The branch director, Zhu Niansheng, opened the court for preliminary interrogation. The wounded soldier gave his name as Zou Chuanyang. Director Zhu took the confession and, considering that the case involved a wounded soldier forcing rape, he could not handle it himself. He sent both parties to the County Public Security Bureau for interrogation. Yesterday, the 22nd Rear Hospital in Huishan Town learned of this and brought Zou Chuanyang back for trial.

Changzhou

All Five District Chiefs Dismissed. Wuyi County Government previously followed orders regarding the training of district chiefs and assistants with poor performance. The district chiefs to be trained include Bao Zongtang, He Bingyi, Huang Gongwang, Wang Qingtong, and Xu Xihua. They were required to report to the province by August 15th. Bao Zongtang and others failed to report to class on time. The Civil Affairs Department, considering that the district chiefs disobeyed orders and voluntarily abandoned their positions, specially ordered County Magistrate Wu to dismiss them all and cancel their qualifications as district chiefs as a punishment. County Magistrate Wu followed the order on the 28th and is currently selecting replacements.

Convict Chen Yuncai Sentenced to Death. On July 29th of this year, Cuiqiao Town in Wuyi County was plundered by bandits, who surrounded a sub-station of the 10th Public Security Bureau, killed sentry He Liansheng, and looted six firearms. The ringleader Chen Yuncai was captured by the Water Police Team. The District Chief Mao transferred him to the Wujin County Court for interrogation. The investigation confirmed him as the main culprit. It has been heard that he has been sentenced to death in accordance with the regulations for punishing bandits.

Jiangyin

Zhu Nan Will Be Sentenced by Military Law. Zhu Xingnan from Xiagang was arrested in Suzhou last month for being involved in a communist case. He used the alias Wang Chuntao. His concubine, Shen Yunzhen, used the alias Wu Qingxi (already sentenced to ten months in prison by the High Court). After Zhu Xingnan was escorted to the Shanghai Songhu Garrison Command, he was then escorted to the Zhenjiang Provincial Security Office. After being interrogated once by Ban Dechang, a staff member of the Second Division and Third Unit of the Provincial School, he was detained in the County Court detention center. Regarding how to handle the case, it is heard that it will be transferred to the Jiangsu Provincial Temporary Military Law Joint Trial for processing.

Nantong

Provincial Security Regiment Searches for Remnant Bandits Along the Coast. The Yanfu area of Jiangbei has been disturbed by Ma Ren's bandit army. Ma calls himself the commander-in-chief of the Pseudo-Punitive 16th Route Army and commander of the 27th Army. The army is said to have four divisions. After the Provincial Security Regiment advanced to suppress them, Ma's army collapsed within a week, rescuing over 200 kidnapped men and women. The regiment is now searching for remnant bandits along the coast in multiple routes and is working with local authorities to handle the aftermath. They are also dispatching teams to protect various salt reclamation companies in collecting crops.

Pinghu

Wu Boying Escapes from Bandits and Returns. Liu Shouquan, a wealthy merchant in Xitang Bridge, was kidnapped by bandits a few days ago and extorted for ransom. At the same time, Wu Boying, the owner of a timber business in Xieqiao, was also kidnapped. It is now known that Wu Boying has safely returned. He stated that one night, a large gang of bandits went out to rob, and the two guards were negligent. They drank and fell asleep. Taking advantage of their unpreparedness, he broke down the door and escaped. A certain agency in the urban area learned of this and has sent people to inquire about everything in order to find ways to rescue Liu Shouquan.

Huzhou

Huzhou-Changxing Night Boat Robbed En Route. The Huzhou-Changxing night boat was traveling from Huzhou to Changxing on the afternoon of the day before yesterday. When it passed the Xiachuqiao area of Lushan, it was already dark. Suddenly, three bandits were seen on the shore, each holding a wooden gun, speaking in a Henan accent, ordering the boat to stop. The boat owner stopped the boat. One bandit kept watch on the shore while the remaining bandits went on board and searched at will. All the silver, money, and belongings of the passengers were robbed, with losses of over one hundred yuan.

Kidnapping and Robbery in Lijia Alley. On the 26th, at around 9:00 PM, a peasant named Jiang Shuiqing's home in Jiangjia Village, near Lijia Alley, Changxing County, Huzhou, was suddenly attacked by a dozen or so bandits speaking in a Henan accent. They held firearms, broke down the door, overturned boxes and chests, and ransacked the place, looting all the clothes, silver, and other belongings. Before leaving, they also kidnapped Shuiqing's nephew and left a letter demanding 3,500 yuan for ransom, specifying a location for contact, otherwise they would tear up the ticket and set the house on fire.

Hangzhou

Statistics on the Export Volume of Local Products. Zhejiang's local products are known for silk, cotton, and tea. According to customs investigations, tea sales have been steadily increasing year by year, while silk and satin have been declining. The quantity statistics are as follows: (1) Silk and satin: 754 dan (approximately 92,000 lbs); (2) Cotton yarn: 26,270 dan (approximately 3,209,210 lbs); (3) Tea: 180,635 dan (approximately 22,097,900 lbs); (4) Silk waste: 20,600 dan (approximately 2,522,700 lbs); (5) Paper: 48,020 dan (approximately 5,878,860 lbs); (6) Vegetable cakes: 175,800 dan (approximately 21,514,800 lbs); (7) Ham: 3,922 dan (approximately 480,174 lbs).

Letters to the Editor

Letter from Wang Meichu of Songjiang

On the 27th, I saw in your newspaper's letter column that Ye Zonglian, the owner of Tai Shun Yuan Rice Store, stated in his letter that I am still working in the store, which does not conform to the facts reported in your newspaper. Meichu has suffered terrible oppression and humiliation, which is more than what was stated in your newspaper's dispatch on the 26th. I was forced to leave the store and originally intended to commit suicide. However, because my parents are still alive and I have not fulfilled my duty as a son, and after being persuaded by my fellow apprentices and brothers who searched and found me, I reluctantly returned to the store that evening. My master had already gone to Shanghai to find me. When the store received the news that I had been found, they reported it to the owner in Shanghai, who was furious. He immediately sent a letter to the original introducer, stating that I had been dismissed and urging him to come and take me back. How could I endure his repeated oppression? The news reported in your newspaper on the 26th is all true. Therefore, I make a special statement and ask that it be published in the letter column so that everyone knows my difficult situation. Then, I will be forever grateful. Respectfully, Wang Meichu, October 29th.

Education News

Important News

Appeal from Teachers and Staff of Various Middle Schools in Jiangsu Province

| Please issue the August and September salaries by the end of this month |

| The Department Director-General Doesn't Need to Be So Arrogant |

| The Salary Management Office Is Occupying a Useless Position |

The Jiangsu Provincial United Association of Teachers and Staff of Provincial Middle Schools declares regarding salary arrears: To all sectors of Jiangsu Province, paternal elders, and fellow citizens: We have endured economic oppression and suffered hardships, with unexpressed grievances for a long time. Now, we can no longer bear it and are about to make a solemn statement. We dare to first share our situation with you, our paternal elders. We have heard that education is the foundation of a nation, the key to its rise and fall, and the cause of order and chaos. Civilized countries around the world, even during times of war, strive to maintain the continuity of teaching. China is unfortunate, with successive disasters. Fortunately, Jiangsu is not a war zone, and schools have not been forced to close. Although we feel that the treatment is not generous and the living conditions are difficult, the burden is heavy, and the work is arduous, we feel that our responsibilities are greater due to the national crisis. We work diligently in teaching and never disobey. We guide and help tirelessly, without seeking comfort. This is to repay the country, inform our paternal elders, comfort the students, and be true to our conscience. Unexpectedly, nearly three months have passed since the beginning of this academic year, and the education funds have not yet been issued. Principals have no means to raise funds and appeal to the authorities. However, the Education Department turns a deaf ear, and the Salary Management Office deliberately obstructs. We deeply understand the difficulties of the times and work on an empty stomach. Even though we are full of wounds and holes, we remain silent. This should be well understood by our paternal elders. However, the salary arrears are increasing day by day, and our suffering is deepening. The cost of living is high, and everything is expensive. Credit is tight, and borrowing is impossible. The funds for supporting our families are essential and cannot be lacking even for a day. As a result, we are willing to serve the public but unable to support our families. If we do not seek other means of survival, we will inevitably sit and wait for death. This is unbearable. Now, the whole province has a great harvest, and everyone is celebrating. The military affairs have ended, and people's lives are stable. The source of education funds is not exhausted. False statements about shortages are aimed at deceiving whom? This is unbearable. The prosperity of education values both talent and resources. Without talent, how can the effect of cultivating talent be achieved? Without resources, it is even more difficult to maintain the function of education. The education officer of a province should recruit talent and entrust them with school administration. They should also plan the economy and avoid hindering progress. However, Director Chen sits high in the hall, and the situation below cannot be conveyed. There are often cases where he refuses to see petitioners, and even more often, he does not approve petitions. He only seeks peace for his ears and does not care about the suffering of the poor scholars. His official demeanor is more than enough, and education is on the verge of bankruptcy. One person's celebration causes worry for the whole province. We are concerned about the future, and our hearts are extremely hurt. This is unbearable. Our Jiangsu education was independent the earliest. Special commissioners were set up for management, and there should be no major problems. Unfortunately, the reception and dispatch of funds are not handled by the right people. As a result, there are many dark secrets, and the economy has not been made public. It takes a lot of effort to investigate and clarify. In the past, when it came to issuing funds on time, there were often delays and suppressions, and some deliberately made things difficult. What is their motive? It is unfathomable. After the start of this academic year, they disregarded the difficulties of the schools and withheld funds, claiming that there was a shortfall. Who can believe such absurd words? Even if it is not false, then what is the duty of these officials? Failure to urge collection is also an inescapable responsibility. If there are many obstacles and collection is indeed difficult, they should step aside and let others take their place. How can they occupy a useless position and cause disaster to Jiangsu? All of this is perplexing and even more strange. The salaries of the officials in the Salary Management Office are issued every half a month. Why are they so loyal to themselves and treat themselves so well? Is there really no one in Jiangsu? This is unbearable. In summary, it is difficult to remain silent. It has been resolved at the 7th Representative Conference of our association that, in addition to submitting a request to the Education Department to order the Salary Management Office to issue the August and September salaries in full by the end of this month, otherwise we will take serious action. We specially state our difficulties and make a solemn declaration. We respectfully ask for your understanding. October 20, 1930.

Ministry of Education Explains the Qualification for Graduation from Training Institutes

The Ministry of Education, based on the report submitted by Chen Yuqi of the Lianhehui (United Association) of Primary and Secondary School Teachers and Staff in An County, Fujian, stated that in the 8th year of the Republic (1919), the Beijing Ministry of Interior established the Local Autonomy Model Training Institute in the capital to prepare for local autonomy. The Ministry of Interior sent a directive to the highest administrative officials in each province and region to select qualified personnel to attend the institute. According to Article 2 of the institute's charter, students must meet the following requirements: (1) Be at least 30 years old; (2) Have graduated from a law and political school for at least one and a half years, or have a background as a Juren (successful candidate in the imperial provincial exams) or Gongshi (successful candidate in the imperial palace exams) or above in the Qing Dynasty, or have held a substantive position equivalent to a recommended or appointed official; (3) Have at least two years of experience in handling local public welfare undertakings; (4) Have not been subject to criminal punishment or declared bankrupt. What kind of school can this training institute be compared to? What kind of qualification does its graduation entail? Is it equivalent to the level of secondary schools? These matters concern qualification issues. The director requests a clear explanation. The Ministry of Education replied: The report has been received. This training institute was originally established to meet a temporary need and is not within the scope of the academic system. It is difficult to compare it to various formal schools, and the qualifications of its graduates cannot be equivalent to those of secondary school graduates. Furthermore, the organization of the Lianhehui of primary and secondary school teachers and staff lacks a legal basis. If the members of the association aim to study education matters and develop local education, they should join the county education association if it has been established. Otherwise, they should submit a request to the county education bureau to organize a county education association in accordance with the regulations of the education association. Please comply accordingly.

Zhejiang Library's New Building Completed

Currently Undergoing Interior Painting

Zhejiang University previously received 200,000 yuan donated by Tang Shouqian to build the Zhejiang Library. It has been a year since the land was found in Pujiang Lane to build the building. It has now been completed. The building was designed and constructed by the Shanghai Yangzi Construction Company. The building is tall and stands upright in the sky, making it quite magnificent and solemn. It is now learned that the interior of the building is currently being painted, and the flower garden outside the building is also being built and equipped. It is expected that it will be fully completed by the end of November. It is also learned that all the libraries of the College of Engineering, the College of Agriculture, and the College of Liberal Arts of Zhejiang University have been instructed by the Secretariat of the university to close and merge. As soon as the building is furnished, an opening ceremony will be held on a scheduled date.

Statistics on Education in Wu County

The Education Bureau of Wu County submitted a report to the county government yesterday on the general state of education for the 19th year. The details are as follows: (1) The total number of school-age children in the county is 157,293; (2) There are 174 county-run primary schools, 26 of which are complete primary schools, with a total of 844 classes; there are also 40 private schools;

(3) The total number of primary school students in the county is 22,499 in county-run primary schools and 4,637 in private schools; (4) The number of secondary schools and students in the county: (A) One county-run junior high school with 246 students; (B) One county-run rural normal school with 165 students; (C) Sixteen private secondary schools with a total of 2,254 students; (5) The total number of teachers in the county: 381 male teachers and 68 female teachers in county-run schools, and a total of 212 teachers in private schools; (6) Financial situation: (A) This year's income is estimated at 590,000, with sources such as the grain transport surtax and universal education land tax, amounting to approximately 286,000 yuan; the deed tax, tooth tax, slaughter surtax, levies from resident households and shop owners, amounting to approximately 134,000 yuan; levies from feasts, Buddhist masses, tin foil, salt tax, and miscellaneous levies, amounting to approximately 53,000 yuan; municipal and county land rent, amounting to approximately 57,000 yuan; tuition fees and subsidies, amounting to approximately 60,000 yuan; (B) Expenditures include 21,000 yuan for educational administration expenses, 96,000 yuan for general education expenses, 323,000 yuan for compulsory education expenses, 85,000 yuan for social education expenses, and 65,000 yuan for other special reserve expenses, totaling 590,000 yuan.

Beijing Academic Society Temporarily Suspends Lectures

The Nanjing Academic Lecture Society held an executive committee meeting at the Ministry of Education the day before yesterday. It was resolved that due to the lack of a public lecture hall in the capital, public lectures are facing many difficulties. The Ministry of Education is currently constructing a lecture hall, which is expected to be completed in about six months. After the completion of the hall, the Academic Lecture Society will continue to hold monthly lectures. The announcement is recorded as follows: To whom it may concern, since its establishment, this society has held monthly public lectures and academic discussions, which have made considerable contributions to culture. Unfortunately, the lack of a public lecture hall in the capital has often caused inconvenience when using temporary venues. The executive committee meeting yesterday resolved that the society's lectures will be temporarily suspended. The Ministry of Education is building a lecture hall, and once the lecture hall is completed, the society will resume holding public lectures. This is hereby announced.

Grand Opening of the Beijing Municipal Women's Vocational School

In order to implement women's vocational education and centralized training, the Beijing Municipal Education Bureau will, starting this semester, convert the four existing women's vocational training classes attached to various municipal schools into a special school, using the old Chong Sheng Temple in the Confucius Temple as the school building. Classes began in mid-September. Due to the convenient location, a large number of students have enrolled. In terms of curriculum, in addition to general education courses, there are courses such as embroidery, flower making, sewing, knitting, and weaving, which are practical and deeply trusted by society. Therefore, a supplementary opening ceremony was held on the 27th of this month. Principal Ma failed to take adequate precautions beforehand and, after the fact, listened only to one side of the story, falsely accusing students Li Xiong and Yan Jingzhao of privately reporting to the military, resulting in their expulsion. However, the perpetrators who caused the disturbance were allowed to attend classes without consequence. Is this fair and just? The actions of a small number of students who caused the disturbance is one matter, while the military's search and arrest of students is another. The former falls within the administrative scope of the school, and Principal Ma should handle it impartially and take appropriate action. The latter involves the Party Headquarters, and Principal Ma should consult with the Party Headquarters and handle it properly to avoid escalating the incident. However, Principal Ma did not do this and instead deliberately showed favoritism, which aroused public anger and offended the Party. Now that the incident has escalated and the situation has suddenly become serious, it is no longer just a matter of inappropriate internal measures but has turned into a matter of offending the Party externally. We and other colleagues, out of love for the school and our fellow students, are unwilling to lag behind in clarifying the truth and upholding justice. In order to save the school and quell the turmoil, we have requested the school authorities to reinstate students Li and Yan in order to appease the people and resolve the matter. We also hope to unite our efforts and reverse the situation. Only by achieving this goal can we face the wrongly accused students Li and Yan, and only then can we show our sincere love for the school. This declaration is hereby made.
