Members of the Chamber of Commerce Held a Discussion Meeting Yesterday

Members to Go to Beijing in Batches

Zhao Jinqing, Director of the Visiting Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, invited members and experts from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to hold a discussion meeting at the Bank Club on the sixth floor of No. 4 Hong Kong Road at 2 pm yesterday. Over fifty people attended including Ye Fuxiao, Qian Xinzhi, Chen Zeqing, Hu Shuhua, Ye Huijun, Lin Kanghou, Li Fuxun, Pan Xulun, Xu Yongzuo, Li Quanshi, Fang Jiaobo, Lao Jingxiu, Rong Zongjing, Wu Yunweng, Zhang Zilian, Lu Zhixue, Wang Yiting, Zhu Yinjiang, Xu Jiqing, Wang Xiaolai, Liu Wanqing, Lu Chengzhang, Tang Jishan, Shi Boan, etc. Chaired by Zhao Jinqing, the chairman first reported the purpose of today's meeting: (1) There are as many as 400 proposals for this chamber of commerce meeting, but the meeting period is only eight days. All proposals will inevitably be merged. It is hoped that you will express your opinions in the discussion meeting and make thorough and adequate preparations so as not to become paper articles. (2) Pay special attention to the proposals that are important and easy to implement. (3) Please determine the time of your departure at this time so as to negotiate with the Ministry of Railways and add vehicles on time. Next, the members decided to go to Beijing in four batches. The first batch was scheduled to leave Shanghai on the night train on the 30th, the second batch was scheduled to leave on the fast morning train at 9 am on the 31st, and the third batch was scheduled to leave on the fast night train on the 31st. The fourth batch plans to take the new plane from the United States to China, but the plane is currently being refueled. If it is not enough time, it will join the third batch and depart together. Then, Zhang Zilian proposed to ask the chairman to send a telegram to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, listing all the proposals separately in the agenda so that there would be sufficient preparation and time could be saved. The chairman agreed to do so. Then, Lu Chengzhang proposed to first total the proposals and then discuss them in groups, and then make a general report after the meeting is closed. Everyone agreed. Next, the chairman read aloud the main points of each proposal: (1) Matters concerning national unemployment relief; (2) Matters concerning industrial relief; (3) Matters concerning international trade; (4) Matters concerning industrial and commercial finance; (5) Matters concerning centralized capital and the use of foreign capital to develop industry; (6) Matters concerning labor welfare and labor-capital disputes; (7) Matters concerning scientific management; (8) Matters concerning commercial tax; (9) Matters concerning industrial raw materials; (10) Matters concerning advocating and protecting domestic products; (11) Matters concerning the improvement of inherent products; (12) Matters concerning basic industry, totaling twelve items. If you have any opinions, you may wish to express them here and notify the ministry first. Then, Zhang Zilian proposed that, in view of the current situation, the proposal that can solve the first matter is to promote domestic products. Therefore, this seat believes that the discussion of the tenth matter proposal should be given special attention. Finally, it was said that the conference should seriously review the proposal itself and not be prejudiced because of the proposer's reputation. Next, Li Quanshi proposed to ask the chairman to telegraph the registration list to the reception office of the conference in advance for contact. The chairman agreed to do so. Next, Xu Jiqing proposed that the suggestions of the members should focus on what is important and easy to implement, and not just sing high tunes. Next, Qian Xinzhi and Pan Xulun successively spoke, requesting the chairman to telegraph Director Zhang of the Secretariat of the Conference and to absolutely refuse entertainment after arriving in Beijing, so as to save time and concentrate on the discussion of the agenda. At most, the conference and the various places outside the conference should be combined for one entertainment, and all others should be rejected. Next, Lin Kanghou reported that Rong Zongjing's temporary proposal was to promote the establishment of a commercial arbitration office as soon as possible, so that merchants' disputes could be resolved by the arbitration office in a few words without legal procedures and spending a long time. Next, Lu Chengzhang asked whether the conference badges would be issued in Shanghai or in Beijing. The chairman replied that they would be issued in Beijing. Next, the chairman declared that the conference would open at 11 am on November 1. If you are leaving Shanghai on the night train on the 31st, please arrive at the station around 10 o'clock so that the greeters can easily greet you. Otherwise, time will be tight and there may be delays. Next, tea and snacks were served and the meeting adjourned at 4 o'clock.

Proposals from Various Parties at the Industry and Commerce Conference

Ren Jinpin Requests the Establishment of a National Products Award Bureau. Many proposals were made by various parties at this National Industry and Commerce Conference. Key points are extracted and recorded below:

Wang Xiaolai (1) Regarding unemployment relief, adopt protective policies, order existing factories not to experience shutdowns or strikes, investigate when factories experience slow sales, and provide government guarantees. Also, encourage the establishment of simple factories to accommodate unemployed workers. (1) Regarding industrial relief, (1) domestically produced cotton should be granted reduced tax rates to facilitate mutual sales. Woven fabrics should especially have taxes reduced to promote sales, emphasizing domestic products. (2) When unavoidable, the tax rate on imported foreign cotton should also be reduced to broadly receive foreign cotton. However, clear regulations should be established to limit this practice, preventing textile factories from closing due to cotton shortages. (1) Regarding industrial relief and international trade, compile and publish annual statistics listing which exported goods are the most prominent to awaken industry and commerce. Pay special attention to which raw materials are processed into finished goods for sale in our country. It is common for domestic products to be transformed into foreign goods. If a fundamental plan can be made to address this issue, starting with a specific product as an experiment and gradually implementing it over the years, the great detriment of exporting raw materials and importing finished goods can be eliminated, not only plugging loopholes but also encouraging industry. (1) Regarding industrial and commercial finance, our country's finance is now centered on banks. The Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Finance should urgently determine the operational areas of each bank, establish regulations, and restrict them from concurrently operating in other industries to align with the true meaning of commerce. (1) Regarding basic industries, expanding provincial roads and developing transportation is a major part of promoting the late Premier's industrial plan. In recent times, many provinces have followed suit. With provincial roads completed, the necessary gasoline and tires are all supplied from abroad. As road administration expands, the import of foreign goods increases. If there is a shortage, transportation will be hindered. The extraction, mining, and refining of our country's oil to supply this essential use is important. Special attention should be paid to this issue, and plans should be made in advance. Not only should the mining and refining of oil not be delayed, but also the purchase and transportation of rubber and the special establishment of factories to imitate tire production is also an important industry. "There are two other jointly proposed items not recorded."

Ren Jinpin. The original site of the old Municipal Hall on Nanjing Road, since being leased by Zhang Zilian and opened as a National Products Joint Emporium, has aroused public sympathy. Recently, the emporium has adopted the "National Products Business Development Plan" proposed by Ren Jinpin and is implementing it in an orderly manner. The departmental organization of the emporium is nearing completion, and large quantities of domestic goods have been purchased for each department. The entire emporium is full of spirit. Commercial leaders Yu Qiaqing and Wang Xiaolai and others express sympathy for Zhang's efforts to fight for national products. Therefore, Ren's "Suggestion for the Government to Establish a National Products Promotion and Award Bureau," submitted to this National Industry and Commerce Conference, has been signed and introduced. The original text is appended below.

Suggestion for the Government to Establish a National Products Promotion and Award Bureau. "Purpose" Implement Article 2 of the National Founding Outline established by the late Premier to enable the government and the people to jointly build the people's livelihood. Adopt methods of awarding national products to encourage commercial organizations specializing in selling national products (such as emporiums and companies) to resist the development of international commerce and realize the fulfillment of the four major needs of clothing, food, housing, and transportation for the people of the country. "Reason" Interpretation of the Premier's Testament. Article 2 of the Premier's National Founding Outline states: (The most important thing in construction is the people's livelihood. Therefore, for the four major needs of clothing, food, housing, and transportation for the people of the country, the government should work with the people to jointly develop agriculture to provide sufficient food, jointly develop weaving to enrich clothing, build various types of houses according to grand plans to provide comfortable housing, and repair roads to facilitate transportation). Is the Premier's intention that the government gather the financial resources of the entire country and have 100 million people weave clothes, 100 million people farm the land, 100 million people build houses, and 100 million people build roads to assist and jointly pursue the welfare of clothing, food, housing, and transportation? This is not the Premier's intention. The Premier's intention is to have the people progress from self-reliance to joint efforts, helping those who help themselves, and supplementing the efforts of joint assistance with the power of the government. Therefore, the initial impetus lies with the people, not with the government. For the people, the first thing is to first exhaust their individual abilities to seek the completion of their individual clothing, food, housing, and transportation, and then seek the completion of their family's clothing, food, housing, and transportation. Secondly, those who have completed their clothing, food, housing, and transportation should seek the comfort of their clothing, food, housing, and transportation, and then help those who have not completed their clothing, food, housing, and transportation to complete it again. Thirdly, those who have quick remedies for clothing, food, housing, and transportation should further help those who are uncomfortable with clothing, food, housing, and transportation to become comfortable and help others who have not completed their clothing, food, housing, and transportation to complete it entirely. "Current Economic Phenomena and Future Perils." Looking around the country today, there are people who have happiness in clothing, food, housing, and transportation, people who have comfort in clothing, food, housing, and transportation, and people who do not have complete clothing, food, housing, and transportation. Then, based on the previous statement, one must assume that those who do not have complete clothing, food, housing, and transportation will soon be able to complete it entirely. This cannot be done daily. Not only will those who do not have complete clothing, food, housing, and transportation not be able to fully complete it, but those who currently have happiness and comfort in clothing, food, housing, and transportation will gradually lose their happiness and comfort and fall into a state of incompleteness. Why do I say this? The completeness of clothing, food, housing, and transportation depends on the production of agricultural and industrial capabilities and the operation of agricultural and industrial capabilities. Promoting agricultural and industrial capabilities for production and operation depends on economic assistance. Without economic assistance, even with agricultural and industrial strength, nothing can be done. Then, what is the current economic phenomenon in China? It is being invaded by foreign commercial policies, with an annual export of 140 million taels, which is nearly 4 million taels per day. Even if it does not increase any further, the total export amount after ten years will be 1.4 billion taels, and the total export amount after two hundred years will be 14 billion taels. Then, the 400 million people of China must each sacrifice their abilities to contribute 35 taels or 350 taels of harvest to foreigners each year in addition to seeking their own livelihoods. I ask, what will be the economic phenomenon in China be like after ten or one hundred years? I am afraid it cannot be asked. Taking a step back, today's economic phenomena in China include unopened mines, uncultivated fields, and unbuilt forests. There are also fields that have been planted but are barren due to a lack of farmers. This is not because China lacks farmers and workers, but because there is a lack of sufficient economy to promote China's agricultural and industrial capabilities to supply the application of opening mines, cultivating fields, and building forests. "The Importance of Implementing Commercial Policies." Therefore, if China wants to enable the 400 million people to fully enjoy the completeness, comfort, and even happiness of clothing, food, housing, and transportation, it must organize resistance to the invasion of foreign economy in commerce. The current era has entered an era of commercial warfare. People are using commercial policies to plot against us daily, and we cannot but use commercial policies to respond to them. Among the organizations of the so-called commercial policies, the most important principle is to enable the nation's merchants to jointly develop foreign trade. Only when foreign trade can develop can domestic industry and domestic agriculture rise. Therefore, in China, where the economy is backward, agriculture and industry are unemployed, foreign goods are abundant, and mines, fields, and forests are abandoned, it is especially necessary to implement commercial policies to seek economic relief and enable the people to enjoy the welfare of clothing, food, housing, and transportation. (Reforming Commercial Organizations and Commercial Policies). We already know that China wants to seek economic relief and enable the people to enjoy the welfare of clothing, food, housing, and transportation, and it is necessary to implement commercial policies. Then, how will the organization of its policies begin? Will the merchants of the country unite to organize it together? Today's Chinese merchants are insufficient to speak of commercial policies. The main work of commercial policies has two major aspects: domestic and foreign. Today's Chinese merchants have long been tempted by the benefits of other countries' commercial policies towards us, and most sell goods from other countries and become organizations that promote foreign commercial policies. It is impossible to expect them to develop foreign commercial policies, and it is also impossible to expect them to work hard for domestic commercial policies. Therefore, we already know the importance of implementing commercial policies, and if we want to plan the progress of commercial policies, we must start by reforming the existing bad commercial organizations. If we want to reform the existing bad commercial organizations, we must engage in the collection of the nation's consumption power and jointly assist commercial organizations that fully promote domestic goods to create a new organization of Chinese commerce. Only then can commercial policies be spoken of. (National Goods Award Bureau and National Goods Stores). If the above-mentioned new organization of commerce can further expand, then it will be seen that all the streets and markets in the country are stores that promote national goods, and there will be no trace of foreign goods in circulation. Then, national goods will increase and develop daily, and agricultural and industrial enterprises will be able to progress together. In this way, the domestic purpose of commercial policies can be fully realized, and then foreign development can be sought. Or if it is said that it can indeed be done according to the aforementioned procedures to achieve the domestic goal of commercial policies, then what techniques will be used to create this new organization of commerce and achieve the so-called domestic goal of commercial policies? It is necessary to devote all efforts to the implementation of the poorly drafted National Products Business Development Plan (see the plan book for details). If this plan can be unimpeded, effective, and the government can find ways to promote the National Products Award Bureau as a strong incentive, then like a tiger and a dragon, the rise of national goods stores will be like spring shoots after rain, and the smooth sale of national goods and the development of agriculture, industry, and hundreds of industries will be like the circulation of the atmosphere, reaching everywhere. (Measures) (1) Imitate the regulations for encouraging afforestation, cotton cultivation, sugar making, and reclamation to award commercial organizations that fully promote national goods (commercial centers, stores, or commercial firms). (2) Imitate the regulations for encouraging overseas Chinese to invest in and establish industry and mining to award people who invest in or initiate commercial organizations that fully promote national goods. (3) Imitate the regulations for awarding inventions and crafts to reward individuals or groups who have made special achievements in promoting national goods and expressing opinions and writings on promoting national goods. (Conclusion) If this is done, then the domestic and foreign work of China's commercial policies will be able to be quickly successful by the people's efforts and the government's rewards. If the domestic work of commercial policies can be completed, then the overflowing loopholes will be plugged, the domestic economy will be prosperous, and foreign trade will also develop accordingly. At this time, continue to work hard, move the remaining strength of domestic work, and seek the direction for foreign countries so that the country's surplus production can travel across the oceans to exchange for foreign currency to plan for the completeness and comfort of the four major needs of clothing, food, housing, and transportation for all the people of China. It is almost certainly the case. Li Kui'an, Standing Committee Member of the National Chamber of Commerce Federation. Li Kui'an, a standing committee member of the National Federation of Commerce, attended the National Industry and Commerce Conference and made many proposals, all of which were important. (1) It is proposed that the government establish an economic guidance organization to guide the production business as the center. (2) It is proposed to implement the recovery of inland river navigation rights. (3) Improve domestic silk to maintain the foundation of the country. (4) Maintain the foreign trade of tung oil. (5) Consolidate southwest finance. (6) Request the government to handle national industrial and commercial statistics. The measures for each of the above cases are extremely thorough. However, due to the length of the words, I cannot record them all. There are several other proposals introduced by Mr. Li. From this, it can be seen that all the attending committee members of this Industry and Commerce Conference are extremely attentive.

Shen Huachen. Two proposals from member Shen Huachen are recorded below. (1) Regarding the development of industry and the protection of domestic goods, it is proposed to legislate to protect domestic fledgling industries and formulate regulations to prevent mergers and taxes. It is imperative to investigate that our country's industry is fledgling, which is the root cause of weakness. If we want to survive, we must protect it with laws. Capitalists of imperialist countries exercise economic aggression and adopt merger policies to destroy our fledgling industry. I will cite two examples to prove this. (1) There are only three cement factories in our country. They are operating miserably and have been repeatedly hit. Today, the domestic construction industry is gradually increasing its need for this. However, Japan is making every effort to destroy it with a merger policy. The selling price of Japanese cement in its own country is 3 yuan and 60 sen per barrel, equivalent to about 4 taels and 7 qian in standard silver dollars. Shipping to China requires an additional shipping fee of 1 tael and 7 qian and 4 fen. The proper selling price per barrel should be 6 taels and 4 qian and 4 fen. However, it deliberately raises the price, below the cost. In May of this year, a Japanese firm sold it to the British Works Bureau for 2 taels and 5 fen, which is a clear proof. (2) The number of Swedish matches sold in China is truly astounding. The set selling price is only half of the cost. This is another proof of the merger policy. If you really want to seek strength and seek the survival of industry, you must legislate protection and implement prevention of merger and tax regulations. I humbly read the late Premier's National Founding Outline, which stated in the industrial plan that to develop China's industry, the government must protect it with laws and regulations. The glorious legacy should be a clear lesson for centuries. We should quickly enact protection laws and clearly stipulate regulations to prevent mergers and taxes to maintain our country's fledgling industry. I am extremely fortunate to present my humble views and respectfully request a decision for implementation. (2) Regarding international trade matters, it is proposed to remove the cocoon tax to reduce the cost of Chinese silk and benefit foreign trade. It is essential to maintain our country's silk industry, which occupies an important position in international trade and has a profound relationship with farmers' and workers' livelihoods. Recently, it has been manipulated by Japanese silk, suspended by European sales, and affected by sluggishness, even to the point of collapse. This is a deep fear for the future of the domestic silk industry. The most important remedy is to reduce the burden and eliminate the cocoon tax. The export of silk must be taxed, and cocoons are the raw material for silk. The cocoon tax is a heavy tax. Moreover, silk is different from other businesses. The success or failure of sales and the high or low market prices are all at the mercy of foreign merchants, and the price of purchased cocoons must be shifted according to the abundance of the year and cannot be taxed according to the silk market. Cocoon prices are too low, which will damage farmers' profits. Moreover, spring, summer, and autumn cocoon harvesting all have fixed times and cannot be estimated in advance. The price of silk sales is used to list the cost of purchasing cocoons. Other industrial products can calculate the selling price based on the cost, but the silk industry has no grasp of either. Based on this argument, eliminating the cocoon tax is the first step to remedy the silk industry. If it is said that it concerns the national budget and is not easy to change, it should be known that tariff autonomy will be implemented in January of the Republic of China in the 20th year, and a strategy of increasing income from import tariff items can be used. Please propose, and I humbly await a public decision. Proposer: Member Shen Huachen.

Zhang Zilian, Shanghai National Products Factory Federation Supervisory Committee Member Zhang Zilian was hired by Minister Kong as a member of the National Industry and Commerce Conference by letter. Mr. Zhang has now collected the opinions of various factories and created proposals. The content (1) of economic preparation is divided into four categories: A, B, C, and D. (A) Negotiate with banking groups to allocate inherent capital. (B) Encourage overseas Chinese to invest in domestic industry. (C) Confiscate public property and transfer it to relieve industry and commerce. (D) Utilize foreign capital to develop domestic industry. (2) Talent training is divided into two categories, Zi and Chou. (Zi) Select existing domestic talents. (Chou) Train future talents. The above two methods are ordered to be six methods. (1) Organize a fund custody office. (2) Adopt scientific management methods. (3) Promote labor-capital cooperation. (4) Shi Zhou Zhongqi, Committee Member of the Jiaoji Railway, Director of the National Qingdao University of Technology

Page 10

College, Zhou Zhongqi, was hired by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and attended the Industry and Commerce Conference in the name of expert member. He has now arrived in Shanghai and will transfer to Beijing to participate in the meeting in the near future. Mr. Zhou is a domestic industrial management expert and has long studied industrial policy, factory management methods, labor issues, and railway management. He once served as a professor at Peking University and Lingnan University. It is heard that this time he has made important proposals on industrial policy and railway freight rates at the Industry and Commerce Conference, and he will also compile the China Power Plan published by the company in the Oriental Magazine last year into a proposal.

Seamen's Pay Raise Issue

Can Be Resolved with Jardine Matheson

The Chinese Seamen's Industrial United General Association yesterday (the 29th) convened representatives from the three departments of sailors, stokers, and stewards at its headquarters to discuss the method of raising salaries for Jardine Matheson seamen. Among those present were Xu Yiliang from the Yan Ying General Agency, Wang Xinkuan from the Navigation Industry Nine Public Associations, Zhang Zaitang from the North Jun'an Public Association, Li Wen from the South Jun'an Public Association, Tang Hesheng from the Lianyi Society, Jin Cangyou, and Wang Yongsheng from the Shanghai Branch. After customary greetings, Chairman Zhao Zhizhi reported, stating briefly that repeated negotiations regarding the pay raise for Jardine Matheson seamen had not yet yielded a satisfactory response. The company only requested Mr. Yu Qiaqing to mediate, and finally agreed to a monthly increase of four yuan per person from September 1st of this year. Whether this can be resolved in this way is still uncertain. Because various Chinese shipping companies have already signed an agreement to first increase four yuan from August 1st of this year, and then increase another two yuan in March of next year, it seems difficult to consider this appropriate by comparison. Therefore, this meeting was called to discuss and expedite the matter. Next, Wang Yongsheng, a guiding committee member from the Shanghai Branch, stated that he had been appointed to discuss and mediate the pay raise for Jardine Matheson seamen with Mr. Yu Qiaqing. He expressed that a pay raise of four yuan from September 1st of this year could be finalized, and requested a public decision. Subsequently, the entire assembly approved the plan and appointed Comrade Wang Yongsheng and Association Secretary Liu Yuzhou to handle it. The meeting adjourned without discussing other matters. According to the above meeting, the pay raise issue for Jardine Matheson seamen can now be resolved.

Jiangsu Province Grain Tribute Additional Levy Issue

County Funds and Property Office Pleads for the People

Qin Xitian, director of the Shanghai County Local Public Funds and Property Management Office, yesterday submitted a document to the National Government Executive Yuan, Ministry of Finance, Jiangsu Provincial Government, and Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance regarding the additional levy on grain tribute. The document stated: "Regarding the additional levy of two yuan on grain tribute, it has been publicly discussed to temporarily comply and pay. Please promptly issue and promulgate the Land Tax Law to uphold the political system and alleviate the people's hardship." It further stated, "This year's additional levy of two yuan on grain tribute has been publicly announced by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance. While it can indeed alleviate the difficulties of the provincial treasury, it increases the burden on the people. There is something unavoidable in saying this. The heavy burden of land tax in the old Suzhou, Songjiang, and Taicang prefectures was truly compelled by the tyranny of autocracy. Now, under the banner of revolution, to imitate the abusive policies of inequality is like adding depth to water and heat to fire. This cannot be a regular method. The land tax is valued at one-hundredth of all taxes, which is the principle of the tax law. Therefore, all counties requesting to collect local fees have been rejected if they exceeded the limit. Now, regardless of the amount of the old tax, a uniform two yuan of silver per picul is levied, which is equivalent to increasing the tax by one jiao and eight fen on each mu of land. This violates the established law and cannot be a regular method. Land with grain tribute has heavy taxes, while land without grain tribute has light taxes. Now, the light ones are not increased, while the heavy ones are made heavier, which is uneven and unreasonable. This cannot be a regular method. The Department of Finance believes that the price of rice has increased, and the conversion rate should be increased accordingly. However, grain tribute is purchased, not levied. This name should not exist in the Republican era. Furthermore, in the autocratic dynasty, the discount on grain prices was limited to eight thousand, and no further increase was allowed. Therefore, warlords resorted to violent extortion and arbitrary taxes under the guise of borrowing grain tribute and dared not openly levy additional taxes. By comparing this case, it not only loses public support but also violates the political system. This cannot be a regular method. The district chiefs of our county previously held a meeting at our office and resolved that they would make efforts to bear the expenses of the provincial treasury. However, they believe this is an expedient measure and definitely not a long-term solution. They requested our office to submit a petition to your government (yuan) (department) (廳), stating that this additional levy should still be carried out temporarily in accordance with the previous temporary additional levy for the Northern Expedition expenses. They also requested that a tax law be formulated and promulgated to various provinces according to land prices. Our office dares not withhold this information and hereby presents it for your review and instruction. This would be a virtuous and convenient act. In addition to submitting it to the National Government (Executive Yuan) (Ministry of Finance) and the Jiangsu Provincial Government, we respectfully present this document. (The following is omitted)."

South Africa Oppresses Overseas Chinese

City Chamber of Commerce Sends Telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Strive for Justice

In recent years, overseas Chinese have been groaning under the oppression of imperialism, with almost no place to stand. Recently, the South African Federal Government has once again excluded Chinese merchants. The City Chamber of Commerce believes that this concerns the lives of overseas Chinese merchants and has sent a telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to strive for justice. The telegram stated: "To the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Nanjing, on the 27th of this month, we received a letter from He Zuan, the acting Consul-General in South Africa, stating that anti-Asian sentiment in the South African Federation is increasing. Recently, they have stopped issuing business licenses to Chinese, which is illegal and violates treaties. Our consulate is striving for justice. In addition to reporting to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, we are sending the original text of the report to the ministry for your review." The South African Federal Government's Transvaal recruited a large number of Chinese laborers when it opened gold mines in the late Qing Dynasty for its use. Afterwards, when the mining operations ended, the miners were sent back one after another and were not allowed to stay. To this day, only merchants remain among the overseas Chinese in that country, and there are no workers. According to the general practice of the United States and Australia to exclude Chinese workers, the South African Federal Government has no excuse. However, it has gone a step further and taken the step of suspending the issuance of business licenses to Chinese merchants in order to implement its private city regulations established in 1907. This means that even a small number of Chinese merchants are not allowed to stand. Even the United States and Australia, which are the most famous for excluding people of color today, do not have such harsh measures. Although the South African Federation is an autonomous colony, it is nominally under the British Imperial Government. Therefore, the friendly and commercial treaty concluded between China and the United Kingdom must be faithfully observed by the Federal Government. This act of violating the treaty and forcing Chinese merchants to close their businesses should be protested severely by your ministry through its ambassador to the United Kingdom. It should also be stated that if the Federation has any actions to promote commerce with China in the future, China must adopt corresponding retaliatory measures before improving its treatment of overseas Chinese. This is because British Canada and other places have been making every effort to promote business in China while at the same time restricting overseas Chinese as much as possible. Our government must express its serious concerns in order to change the British attitude. This is not only for the South African Federation but for all British territories. Is this appropriate? We request your review and instruction."

Postal Items Will Now Be Forwarded Via Siberia

Except for Those Specifying Surface Mail

According to the Shanghai Postal Authority, there have been important changes in the way postal items are forwarded via Siberia. Previously, postal items were not forwarded via Siberia unless the sender specifically indicated it. Now, starting from the 29th of this month, all postal items addressed to the following locations will be forwarded via Siberia, unless the sender specifies otherwise. The postal notice is as follows: "All postal items from all parts of China to Europe, northern and western Africa, Turkey, and South America (Panama, Colombia, Venezuela, Peru, Bolivia, and Ecuador, except for those shipped via Japan and the Pacific route) will be sent via the Siberian route, unless they specify via the Suez Canal or the United States."

Pitiful Old Farmer Bitten by a Mad Dog

Comes to Shanghai Seeking a Cure

Tang Agen, a 29-year-old villager from outside the South Gate of Jiading, has been farming for a living. He has an ox at home to plow the fields. On the afternoon of August 29th (lunar calendar), Tang was leading the ox to graze in the fields. At noon, while the ox was eating grass, a mad dog suddenly ran wildly, bumping east and west. There happened to be another old farmer, about 50 years old, in the field, carrying a hemp bag and sitting on the ground. Unexpectedly, the mad dog ran up and bit the hemp bag, instantly tearing a hole. The flesh on the old man's foot was also torn by the teeth, causing extreme pain and bleeding. Tang intended to lead the ox away, but the mad dog pounced again and bit the ox's foot. The ox, in extreme pain, stumbled and fell into the ditch. Tang, in order to protect the ox, used his whip to strike the dog but was bitten by the dog in his left foot near the small toe, creating a hole the size of two hao coins, with blood dripping. Although he managed to return home, both Tang and the ox walked with difficulty, with intermittent bleeding. They repeatedly sought medical treatment, but it was not effective. Tang later learned that a villager named Wang outside the North Gate had also been bitten by a mad dog and died this month due to lack of treatment. As a result, he was extremely worried. He came to Shanghai from his hometown on the morning of the day before yesterday and is staying with a fellow villager in the French Concession. He intends to seek a cure from all walks of life in order to recover. Tang is in dire straits and lacks the funds to seek a famous doctor. He is extremely anxious and hopes that all sectors, if they have a good remedy for mad dog bites, will immediately inform him at Gong's residence, 22 Yuan Shang Li, Ningbo Road, French Concession, which would also be a charitable act.

Note: Yu Liangxin Pharmacy at the entrance of Shi Jia Lane in the city and Lao Zhenghe Dye House east of Zhengjia Wood Bridge on Avenue Edward VII both have this remedy.

Scavenging Child Crushed to Death by a Truck

At 4:00 PM on the day before yesterday, a truck carrying kiln goods was driving to Zhongshan Road north of Xiaoshadu Creek. A 10-year-old Yancheng boy named Qi Wuneng, who was scavenging, was walking in the road. He was unable to avoid the truck and was knocked down. The wheels crushed his abdomen, causing his liver and intestines to spill out. He died instantly in a terrible state. The truck driver was arrested by the police on duty and taken to the police station for detention. Yesterday, Zhang Xietang, the head of the Twelfth District in the north, reported the incident to the local court for inspection.

Over a Thousand Cases of Gasoline Burned

Huidefeng Tugboat Was Careless

Extinguished After Three Quarters of an Hour

Yesterday at 1:30 PM, a fire broke out in the middle cabin of the Huidefeng tugboat, which was loaded with over 6,000 cases of gasoline, at the De Tu Gu kerosene depot at 101 Yangshupu Road. In an instant, smoke filled the sky and sparks flew everywhere. The Yangshupu Fire Brigade drove fireboats to spray water and extinguish the fire, which took three quarters of an hour to extinguish. Fortunately, it was raining heavily, and only over a thousand cases were burned.

Financial Bureau Publishes Business Report for the 17th Year

"Shanghai Finance" Quarterly to Be Published as Well

The Shanghai Financial Bureau compiles and publishes a business report every year after the end of each year, which is distributed and sold separately as a reference for those who care about municipal finance. Now, the bureau's business report for the 17th year has been published. It contains detailed records of the administration and various plans and regulations for the year 17, with extremely rich content. In addition to the bureau distributing it to various organizations and groups and selling it, it has also entrusted the Commercial Press, China Great Eastern World Bookstore, and other bookstores in this port to sell it on its behalf to facilitate the purchase by citizens. It is heard that the first issue of the "Shanghai Finance" quarterly, which is compiled by the Bureau's Publications Editorial Committee, will also be published soon.

Reverend Xue of the Apostolic Church Passes Away

The Mainland Daily reported that Reverend Xue of the Apostolic Church, Rev. Father R. P. Chevalier, suddenly passed away on the 27th at the Yangjingbang Catholic Church. Father Xue came to China at a young age and first preached in the interior. Later, he presided over Xuhui Public School for 20 years and especially supported the observatory. Recently, due to his old age and weak health, he relinquished his heavy duties and retired to the Yangjingbang Catholic Church. He was a highly respected elder in the Catholic Church. Unfortunately, he succumbed to illness and passed away at the age of 78.

Luo Chung Court Teahouse and Bookstall Are Full

Since the opening of the new bookstall in the Luo Chung Court Teahouse on Zhejiang Road, there has been no vacant seat day and night. The location is appropriate, and the storytellers are all famous. It is also heard that from today, Shen Jianan and Si Xiaoqing will be added to the stage every night to sing and tell stories.

Snake Eater at the Great World

The strange man Hailancha is able to swallow all kinds of poisonous snakes, birds, and insects alive. He has never eaten human food. It is heard that the Great World believes that this strange man has great appeal and can add color to the business. Therefore, it has made every effort to persuade him to perform on stage, and he is scheduled to perform on stage today. It is also heard that the strange man said that for this performance, he will invite people from all walks of life to bring various poisonous animals to eat alive on the spot.

Yuyuan Merchants Organize National Products Promotion Association

The merchants of the Yuyuan Temple area have initiated the organization of a National Products Promotion Association, which has been approved by the Municipal Citizens Training Association and issued a license for preparation. The preparatory committee has been established, consisting of Zhu Jueying, Yang Zhitian, Shi Xiaoshan, Li Rongsen, Zou Gengfu, Gu Liansheng, Zhou Rongchang, Zhang Yinkui, Liu Chuntai, Hu Xuegeng, Zhao Buchen, Chen Yunji, Shen Chunrong, Huo Lansheng, Zhang Yushan, Hu Wenhan, Ni Qilin, Hu Jiajun, Lu Gensheng, Fang Dequan, and Chen Jixiang, totaling 21 people. Water and Electricity Workers Union: The preparatory committee of the Federation held its 12th standing committee meeting yesterday. Chairman Hu Peiji discussed: (1) Regarding the case of how the union should handle the registration forms submitted by affiliated unions, which only have one copy filled out, it was resolved that the union should make three copies itself for reference. (2) The standing committee mentioned that the living expenses for employees of the union for September have not yet been fully paid, and October is approaching. It is feared that the employees will not be able to work with peace of mind, which will hinder the progress of union affairs. How should this be addressed? It was resolved to ask the instructor to explain the situation to the city party headquarters, requesting that the subsidies for September and October be issued together to benefit the union's affairs.

Western-Style Furniture Workers Union: The first standing committee meeting was held yesterday, chaired by Zhou Maoshan. The ceremony was performed, oaths were taken, and reports were given (summary omitted). Job assignments were allocated, and Huang Zhengzhong, Yuan Fuyun, and Zhao Daolin were publicly elected as standing directors. Huang Zhengzhong was mutually elected as the resident standing director, Hong Zongliang as the director of the organization section, Zhou Maoshan as the director of the training section, Zheng Yongshou as the director of the publicity section, and Yuan Fuyun as the director of the general affairs section. Huang Zhengzhong also served as the director of the mediation section. Discussions: (1) A letter was received from the trade association stating that Chen Songmao had dismissed two workers, Zhou Rongcai and Feng Dexing, both of whom are responsible personnel of the union. How should this be handled? It was resolved to reply to the trade association, ordering them to share the work to avoid unemployment. If they do not comply, a request will be submitted to the government to penalize them for deliberately undermining the union. (2) Chen Songmao fired worker Ruan Zicai a long time ago and refused to pay him wages for the Revolutionary Memorial Day. How should this be handled? It was resolved to order Ruan to ask for the wages again. If they are still withheld, a request will be submitted to higher authorities for severe punishment. (3) How should members on duty be punished for absenteeism without cause? It was resolved that those who are absent once or intermittently twice will be questioned; those who are absent twice or intermittently three times will be warned; those who are absent three times or intermittently four times, or who do not respond or come to the meeting to explain their reasons, will be fined ten yuan for public use, in addition to requesting higher authorities to dismiss them from their positions. (4) How should the date and time of the standing committee meetings be determined? It was resolved that the meetings will be held twice a month, on the 14th and 29th of each month, at 7:30 PM. (5) Worker Mao Quantai demanded 100 yuan in compensation for a labor dispute, but refused to pay the fee. Mediation has been ineffective after six attempts. How should this be handled? It was resolved to conduct a seventh mediation. If he still refuses to pay, a request will be submitted to higher authorities for severe punishment. (6) Should a joint meeting of labor and management representatives be held to coordinate labor-management relations? It was resolved to first ask the trade association to schedule a date and submit a request to higher authorities for guidance to facilitate the process. (7) How should the monthly salary of the resident standing director be determined? It was resolved to pay a monthly salary of 25 yuan. (8) Alternate director Zhu Bingyao requested leave of absence. Should a replacement be appointed? It was resolved to appoint Feng Dexing to attend the meetings and perform the duties of the duty rotation.

Local News Two

Yuan Shunwu Escapes Danger

Bandit Leader Asks About Yuan's Family Situation

Gun Placed Against His Temple

After Police Investigation

Living God of Wealth Rescued from Empty House

Yuan Shunwu, a student at Datong University who was kidnapped and held in a bandit den for five days for a ransom of 400,000 yuan, was rescued at 5:00 AM yesterday at the end of Yangshupu Road. Yuan was kidnapped on Zhongshan Road on Saturday evening. The bandits sent a letter demanding 400,000 yuan for his release. Fortunately, under the direction of District Chief Ren of the Sixth District Public Security Bureau and the officers Xu and Wei, along with Detective Liu, the bandits were investigated and arrested. Six kidnappers were captured, and the hostage was safely rescued. However, while Yuan Shunwu was in the bandit den, the bandits guarding him addressed him as the God of Wealth and Old Master. Once the God of Wealth broke through the wall and flew away, the bandits' misfortune was also at its peak.

Hostage Hidden in Empty House: After Yuan Shunwu was kidnapped on the 24th, he was sent by the bandits to an empty house at the intersection of Jungong Road at the end of Yangshupu Road to be hidden. This house originally belonged to a flour mill and has been vacant for a long time, attracting no attention, so the hostage was hidden there. After five days, he was found by the Sixth District Public Security Police at 5:00 AM yesterday. Initially, the Sixth District Public Security Bureau detained a suspect in this case, Zou Yaodong from Hubei, at 1213 Han Bi Li Road in the Public Concession. He was taken back for interrogation and confessed that his fellow villager, Xiao Jianxing, was an accomplice in the case. As a result, Xiao and his wife, Ms. Yu, were also arrested. Then, Fang Dewen, Yi Peihan, and Liu Changming were arrested in succession. Liu confessed the location of the hostage in Yangshupu.

God of Wealth Rescued: At 5:00 AM yesterday, the Sixth District Police, along with an informant, rushed to the hostage location at the intersection of Jungong Road at the end of Yangshupu Road. At that time, it was still dark, and it was raining. A Western-style house could be vaguely seen in the dark. The detectives immediately turned on their electric torches and went straight to the house, breaking down the door. No one was found. They searched the rooms near the door first, but found nothing. Then, they passed through two narrow alleys and saw a row of houses, all with closed doors. In the most remote and dark place, they called out Yuan's name and heard a response. They broke down the door and saw the hostage Yuan Shunwu lying on the bed. The bandit guard had escaped without a trace, leaving only three pistols. At this time, Yuan was wearing a shirt on his upper body and suit pants on his lower body. He was in good spirits. Yuan said that there were four bandits guarding him, day and night, calling him the God of Wealth and Old Master, and treating him well with food, drinks, and tea. They even bought books for him to read when he wanted to. What was unbearable was that when the bandit leader asked about his family situation, the bandit held two guns, pointing the muzzles directly at his temples, making him feel uneasy and disturbed.

Case Investigation: After Yuan Shunwu was kidnapped, the bandits sent letters to Datong University three times, demanding 400,000 yuan. During the last letter reception, the Sixth District Public Security Bureau had already arrested Zou Yaodong and Xiao Jianxing, and the investigation was progressing smoothly. On the 28th, it was learned that the accomplices Fang Dewen and others were hiding in Room 38 of the Tongyi Hotel on Liu Ma Road in the Public Concession. District Chief Ren of the Sixth District Public Security Bureau ordered Officers Xu Tao and Wei Jiechen, along with Detective Team Leader Liu Shaoqing, to go there at 4:00 PM and wait in another room. At 11:30 PM, the kidnapper Fang Dewen returned to the Tongyi Hotel and was lured into the room where the detectives were staying to talk. Fang realized that the situation was not good and offered 150 yuan to bribe the detectives. The detectives pretended to cooperate and unexpectedly arrested Fang. Under interrogation, he confessed the location of the hostage, but only his accomplice Liu Changming knew the location. So they rushed to Ninganfang on North Zhejiang Road and arrested Liu.

No Time to Put on Pants: Liu Changming was hiding in the fourth house in Ninganfang on North Zhejiang Road. The detectives of the Sixth District Public Security Bureau first notified a police station in the Fourth District before proceeding to arrest him. It was around 2:30 AM yesterday. The bandit Liu heard someone coming and jumped out of bed, not even having time to put on his pants. He ran naked to the [missing text] house and hid under the bed behind the living room. After Liu was arrested, he confessed the location of the hostage. The Sixth District Police then joined the police of the Fifth District Public Security Bureau in Zhabei and rushed to Yangshupu overnight to rescue the hostage.

Declaration by Various Municipal Party Committees on the Xiao Case

The Shanghai Municipal First Enlarged Propaganda Conference issued a declaration regarding the case of Ms. Xiao Xin'an being humiliated, stating (summary omitted): The cruelty of the imperialists from Japan, the United States, France, Italy, and other countries towards oppressed peoples is no less than that of Britain. In recent years, the Chinese nation has suffered greatly from the oppression, exploitation, humiliation, trampling, and killing by imperialists. Dr. Sun Yat-sen, the leader of our party, could not bear to see our 400 million Chinese compatriots perish, so he raised his arms and carried out the revolution, hoping to break free from the shackles of the imperialists and build a democratic, people-owned, and people-enjoyed Republic of China that would stand permanently in the world. Unfortunately, in the 1911 Revolution, the comrades of our party did not abide by the revolutionary oaths and did not follow the leader's proposals, so the revolutionary strategies were not implemented, and the revolutionary ideology could not be realized, creating a situation of fragmentation and popular suffering for more than ten years, giving all the imperialists the opportunity to gain an inch. At present, the comrades of our party have awakened from the pain. Since the Northern Expedition in 1926, all the reactionary forces in the country have been gradually eliminated, and we could have shifted our focus to actively attack the imperialists. However, for the past three years, newly emerging warlords have rebelled, allowing the rampant imperialists to survive. Thinking of this, how can we not be saddened? Recently, Ms. Xiao Xin'an went to Southeast Asia to educate our overseas Chinese children. Unfortunately, she was raped by the chief mate and second mate of the Zha Hua Shipping Company's ship, the "Zhi Bate." This is a rare and great humiliation in history and in the world. This is not just the animalistic behavior of the chief mate and second mate of the "Zhi Bate," but it fully reveals the entire sinister face of the imperialists. This is not just the humiliation of Ms. Xiao Xin'an, but it is a rare and great humiliation for the entire Chinese nation and all oppressed peoples in the world. This is tolerable, but what is intolerable? We hope that all compatriots in the country will unite and fight a life-and-death battle with the imperialists. If imperialism is not overthrown, China's sovereignty will not be complete, China's independence and freedom will not be achieved, and the life and happiness of the Chinese nation will not be guaranteed. For now, we can only urge the government to submit serious negotiations to the Zha Hua Shipping Company, (1) severely punish the chief mate and second mate of the "Zhi Bate," (2) compensate Ms. Xiao for her reputation damage, (3) formally apologize to our country, and (4) guarantee that similar incidents will not happen again in the future. On the other hand, we should swear not to ride the Zha Hua Shipping Company's ships again in the future, and automatically raise capital to establish shipping companies to recover the rights and protect the safety of overseas Chinese. This is our declaration. Shanghai Special Municipal First Enlarged Propaganda Conference.

Kidnapping and Robbery Combined Sentenced to Death

The kidnapper Zhang Jiarong (also known as Xiao Zhang), on April 5th of last year, colluded with others to hold weapons and break into Yuan Wanlong's auto shop at 1332 Yangshupu Road, kidnapping Yuan's four-month-old son Genwan, and demanding a ransom of 7,000 yuan. He also colluded with others to hold weapons and rob a large amount of valuables from the Jufeng Pawnshop on Yangshupu Road. The General Police Department cracked the case and, along with suspects Yan Deyi, Kan Xijiang, Tao Jinzhi, and Wang Guanzhai, turned them over to the former Provisional Court for trial and detention. Later, the court was reorganized into a special court, and Zhou Tingzhang re-examined and concluded the case. Yesterday morning was the date for sentencing. Judge Zhou Hanting announced the verdict: Zhang Jiarong was sentenced to death for the crime of kidnapping for ransom, and sentenced to 12 years of imprisonment for the crime of robbery at the Jufeng Pawnshop on Yangshupu Road, to be executed by death. The other parts of the indictment were found to be not guilty. Yan Deyi, Kan Xijiang, Tao Jinzhi, and Wang Guanzhai were all found not guilty. The police department lawyer, Ru Baoyi, requested that Yan Deyi be kept in custody during the appeal period, which the court granted.

Special District Local Court to Burn Narcotics Tomorrow

To Be Held at Yizhong Cemetery on North Zhejiang Road

Since its establishment on April 1st, the Special District Local Court has confiscated narcotics such as opium. The court burned them publicly at the end of July. In the past three months, it has confiscated quite a bit more. Now, President Yang of the court has scheduled the second public burning for 2:30 PM on the 31st of this month, again at the Baoan Hall Yizhong Cemetery on North Zhejiang Road. Letters have been sent to various agencies, inviting them to send representatives to supervise the event. The types and quantities of the narcotics to be burned are listed below: (1) 522 pounds of raw opium, plus 519 ounces, plus 19 small pieces, plus 183 small packets, plus 9 small boxes; (2) 9 pounds of opium paste, plus 14 ounces, plus 162 small cans, plus 2 small boxes, plus 3 small jars, plus 2 small cans, plus half a small can; (3) 180 opium pipes; (4) 100 pounds of red pills, plus 7 ounces, plus 660 pills, plus 10 cans, plus 39 small packets, plus 4 small boxes; (5) 119 small packets of morphine; (6) 12 ounces of heroin; in addition, there are 1,711 pieces of smoking paraphernalia and other miscellaneous items, with small amounts of opium ash and opium paste counted as one item each. The value of the above-listed narcotics at current prices is substantial.

Mei Ya Fashion Exhibition

Opening at the Great China Hotel This Afternoon

Dozens of Outfits Showcased by Chinese and Western Ladies

Mei Ya Silk Weaving Factory is a national enterprise, entirely managed by Chinese. Established in Shanghai for ten years, it produces over 500 kinds of products, with annual sales reaching 5 million yuan. Its georgette, crepe satin, Paris crepe, single crepe (commonly known as Indian silk), double crepe, and various types of silk, satin, and tweed are sold to Europe, America, Southeast Asia, India, and various parts of China. This year marks its tenth anniversary. In addition to donating a large number of valuable products to participate in the National Goods Fashion Exhibition on October 9th, which was highly praised by society, it has been decided to hold a special tea dance fashion exhibition at the Great China Hotel at 4:00 PM today to commemorate the tenth anniversary. Invitations have been sent to various sectors of the Party, government, military, business, academia, newspapers, and famous ladies at sea to attend and observe. It is reported that Mayor Zhang of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and Director Pan Gongzhan of the Bureau of Social Affairs will attend and give speeches. The fashion show will be performed by Chinese and Western ladies. The opening ceremony details are previewed below.

Venue Arrangement: The venue is the grand ballroom of the Great China Hotel. All the interior and exterior decorations were designed by Zhong Huang, an expert in architecture and decoration who studied in France, and contracted to Mei Yi Architectural Decoration Foreign Firm. Modern patterns from 1930 were used throughout. A circular stage was built in the ballroom, connected by a movable long bridge, so that the entire audience can clearly see the fashion show without any obstruction. In the center of the stage is a silk-covered electric umbrella lamp, illuminating the entire venue and adding to its novelty and ingenuity. The music stage and the main entrance also have magnificent streamer doors. Siemens has installed the latest telephonic broadcasting equipment in the venue to broadcast music, singing, and speeches throughout the venue, clearly audible everywhere.

Opening Ceremony Program: (1) Opening Ceremony; (2) Party Song; (3) Opening Remarks by General Manager Cai; (4) Speeches by Celebrities; (5) Fashion Show; (6) Tea Dance; (7) Entertainment (Mr. Nicola's Sea Market Madness); (8) Fashion Show; (9) Tea Dance; (10) Entertainment (Cai Ni's siblings, Youthful Play); (11) Fashion Show; (12) Film (Mei Ya Silk Factory's "Chinese Silk," over 2,000 feet long); (13) Music; (14) Refreshments, Adjournment.

Fashion Show Program: Various fashions will be showcased, all made from Mei Ya Factory's own woven and dyed georgette, crepe satin, single crepe, double crepe, and other high-quality silks and satins, specially designed and tailored by Hongxiang Company. The program includes dozens of sets of outfits, including sleepwear, underwear, fashionable cheongsam, garden party dresses, casual wear, outerwear, tennis wear, tea dance dresses, and evening gowns, to be modeled by Chinese and Western ladies.

French Concession to Suspend Electricity Supply for Two Days

Due to Route Repair Work

The French Concession Electric Light Company will suspend electricity supply from today (the 30th) to tomorrow (the 31st), from 7:00 AM to 5:00 PM each day, to repair sections of the route. However, electricity will be provided as usual in the evenings. The affected areas are: (1) Ximen Road, from Sapoxian Road to Belle Road; (2) Baille-Nimma Lang Road, from Puhai Road to Lafayette Road; (3) Wangzhi Road, from Saposey Road to Belle Road; (4) Lafayette Road, from Saposey Road to Baille-Nimma Lang Road. The surrounding areas of the above four addresses will not have electricity because the entire route needs to be repaired and replaced. The company has posted notices on all major thoroughfares to inform the public.

Shanghai Pudong Ferry Offers Preferential Rates to Municipal Government Employees

Special First-Class Round-Trip Tickets Counted as One-Way

The Shanghai Public Utilities Bureau, which operates the Pudong Ferry, has renewed its appearance since the new ferries began operating. People in Shanghai often take the ferry to Pudong during their leisure time to enjoy the scenery and improve their health. In order to encourage employees of the Municipal Government to change their environment, recuperate, and improve their health, the bureau has introduced special preferential measures for ferry rides: (1) Round-trip fares will be charged as one-way fares, with a stamp on the ticket for identification, limited to special first-class cabins; (2) The dates are limited to Sundays and other holidays. Special circumstances require prior agreement from the bureau (such as illness and recuperation, etc.); (3) Each employee can purchase tickets for up to five people per trip, including accompanying family members. The employee must accompany the family members and purchase tickets with their employee ID. It is reported that the above measures have been approved by the Municipal Government and will be implemented from November.

The Shanghai YWCA Labor Department held a social event for women workers at its new location on Nanjing Road the other day. Over 100 members attended and participated in various games, including dances and short plays, all aimed at improving the lives of women workers and enhancing their moral and intellectual qualities, in order to increase the professional skills that women workers deserve. In addition to the classes taught within the group every week, teaching practical crafts, civics, and professional skills, the department plans to invite speakers to lecture on "hygiene" and the "morality" that workers should possess.

Extortion by Threat and Forcing the Writing of "Fu Xi"

To Show Sincere Negotiation

Three Bandits Arrested After Police Report

At the Rong Sheng Xiang cigarette and paper shop, located at No. 287 Tokyo Road, Shanghai West, and owned by Mrs. Feng Zhang from Ningbo, on the 28th of last month, a threatening letter was received from a gang via the post office, demanding 2,000 yuan. It stated that if there was a sincere intention to negotiate, a red paper slip with the characters "Fu Xi" should be posted on the glass window outside the shop counter as a sign. Mrs. Feng reported the letter to the Putuo Road police station in charge and requested an investigation. Subsequently, Mrs. Feng Zhang received three more letters in succession, but each letter was sent by someone dispatched by the gang. On the 27th of this month, at 7 p.m., Mrs. Feng received another letter, instructing her to place the money in a British-brand cigarette box between 12 noon and 1 p.m. the following day and deliver it to the spot behind the British candle factory on Binlang Road, where there was a white paper pasted on the wall, and someone would come to collect it. Mrs. Feng reported this to the police station again. At around 12 noon the day before yesterday, detective Ji Liren, detectives Ma Zonglai, Qi Mengqing, patrolmen Li Shugui, Cui Yulou, and Shao Fuhai, disguised themselves and waited in the nearby sheds. Mrs. Feng sent her shop assistant, Zhang Qiqing, to deliver the British-brand cigarette box on time. Before long, four people were seen lingering in the area for a long time and then approached Zhang to speak with him. The detectives rushed out and arrested them. Unexpectedly, the four bandits scattered and fled. Two of them, Wang Liancheng and Zhou Xiaoerzi (19 years old), both from Jiangbei, were captured on the spot, along with the cigarette box, and taken to the police station. The other two escaped. Later, Zhou Xiaoerzi confessed that the two who escaped were a Mr. Gu and Xu Gengcheng. Gu lived at No. 175 Binlang Road, and Xu lived at No. 131 on the same road. Chinese and Western detectives went to the addresses to make arrests, but only Xu Gengcheng, also from Jiangbei and only 15 years old, was apprehended. Gu's whereabouts were unknown. The police chief ordered him to be detained as well. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Second Criminal Court of the Special District Court. The police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, stated the case and said that the police were still investigating the threatening letters, so he requested an extension. Patrolman Li Shugui also reported the details of the breakthrough. Mrs. Feng Zhang, the plaintiff, also stated that four years ago, she opened the Yichang Xiang cigarette and sundry shop on Moganshan Road and was robbed, with gunfire used as a warning. Later, her shop was destroyed by fire, and she received several hundred taels in fire insurance compensation from the insurance company. Soon after, she received five threatening letters, the first of which mentioned the robbery and compensation. She requested an investigation. When questioned, Wang Liancheng confessed that the matter was done by the fugitive Mr. Gu, and he had delivered letters for him. Yesterday, Gu had also asked him to collect the cigarette box. Zhou and Xu also confessed that they had gone together yesterday but knew nothing else. Judge Wu Tingqi verified the confessions and ordered the three defendants to be remanded in custody pending further investigation at a later date.

Kidnappers from Xinchang Arrested in Shanghai

Jin Jiulin, a detective inspector from the Special Agency of the French Police, detectives Li Yaolong, Qian Yumin, patrolmen Zhou Buguang, Zhang Ziying, and others, recently learned that there were kidnappers at No. 16 Yu Kang Lane, Pishao Nai Road. They went to arrest five men and women: bandits Zhou Shuntang, Zhu Gaosheng, Chen Ziyao, female bandit Zhou Qiusi, and Zhu Husi. They were taken to the police station. When questioned by the police chief, the bandits confessed that they had kidnapped Zhang Kunhua, the owner of a southern goods store, outside the east gate of Yancun Village in their hometown of Xinchang County, Zhejiang Province, earlier this year and released him after receiving a ransom. They had only been in Shanghai for a short time and had not committed any crimes. The police chief, upon receiving this confession, ordered them to be detained. Yesterday, they were escorted to the French Court for interrogation. First, the Western Detective Chief, Sa Cai'er, reported the previous situation. After a brief interrogation by the Chinese and Western officials, they were ordered to be remanded in custody pending a reply from Xinchang County.

Abuse of Wife, Selling of Daughter, and Disrespect to Elderly Mother

Cao Wanfu Sued by His Wife

Requesting Court to Order Divorce

Mrs. Cao Liu, from Yangzhou, was betrothed to Cao Wanfu, a fellow villager, by her parents at a young age, and she immediately became a child bride. Because her husband did not engage in proper work and was devoted to gambling and dissipation, his mother, who was over sixty years old, had to work as a servant to provide for his squandering. This year, he sold his own daughter into a brothel. Mrs. Liu was repeatedly abused and could not bear the suffering. She retained lawyer Song Shixiang to file a lawsuit with the District Court for a divorce to save her life. The gist of her complaint was that the defendant was disrespectful to his parents, sold his daughter, and abused his wife. His conscience was extinguished, and it was difficult to live with him until old age. The plaintiff was betrothed to the defendant by her parents at the age of seven and immediately became a child bride. She married him in the village the following year. Later, the defendant went out to work as a cook but did not engage in proper work and was devoted to gambling and dissipation, abandoning his mother and wife and ignoring his family. The following year, she gave birth to a son, and the family burden became heavier. She relied entirely on her own labor to support the family. Before long, she gave birth to another son. Unable to make a living in the village, she came to Shanghai with her sixty-one-year-old mother to seek work. Her elderly aunt now works as a servant at the Xin Kang Lane, Da Tong Road, Xinzha, and her hard-earned money is squandered by the defendant. The plaintiff initially worked in a Shanghai cotton mill, but because she could not bear the defendant's harassment for money, the factory dismissed her. She then became a servant, but within a few months, she was harassed by the defendant, and the employers, fearing his violence and potential accidents, dismissed her. She changed jobs several times but never had a stable life. Before the Dragon Boat Festival this year, the defendant, due to debt, cruelly sold his six-year-old daughter, Xiaomei, into a brothel and used the money for gambling. When the plaintiff found out and tried to reason with him, she was brutally beaten, covered in injuries, and slandered. She was bedridden for several days. Under these circumstances, the affection was obviously broken. She requested a divorce in accordance with the law. Yesterday morning, Judge Guo Shouyi opened the court for trial. The plaintiff, Cao Liu, recounted the previous situation and requested that the court examine the scars on her arms from the beatings. When questioned, Cao Wanfu claimed that all the plaintiff's allegations were false, and he had not committed any acts of violence and did not want a divorce. Prosecutor Wang attended the court and expressed his opinions. The debate then began. The judge considered the arguments concluded and set the judgment date for the 31st of this month.

New-Style Ford Luxurious Roadster

The Ford Motor Company's new range of luxurious vehicles, including sedans, large cars, and small cars, have arrived in China. Recently, a luxurious roadster has also been shipped. Its mechanics are the same as the new-style Ford, but the unique features are the low, sleek lines and the higher sides of the carriage, deeper seats, and meticulous workmanship throughout. The spacious seats are upholstered in genuine leather, and the top is covered in tan rubberized material, which is easy to fold. The rear seat is also covered in genuine leather. Other advantages include shatterproof glass windshields and wind deflectors, a canopy frame, a spare tire mounted on the mudguard outside the driver's seat, an electric glass wiper, and stainless steel headlamps.

The Scandal of the Female Bus Conductor

Xia Xiuying and Wu Dan

Li Qiaosheng Catches Them in Adultery

Xia Xiuying, a female conductor on the Shanghai South Public Bus, recently fell in love with a passenger, Wu Dan, and eloped with him, lodging in the Datong Hotel. Unexpectedly, Xiuying's husband, Li Qiaosheng, found them and brought them to the First Sub-Bureau of the First District to file charges. The details are recorded below: Xia Xiuying is from Ningbo, is just over twenty years old, and is quite beautiful. Her father, Dinghua, rents a house at No. 65 Nanmatou Street. In April of the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, Xia Xiuying, through the introduction of matchmaker Xie Xuekang, was betrothed to Li Qiaosheng, from Nanjing. In January of the following year, they married and lived together at No. 327 Nanzhan Road. Li Qiaosheng, now twenty-five years old, works as a conductor No. 298 at the French Tram Company. His monthly income is meager, and the household expenses are often tight. Since Xiuying married into the family, the relationship between the two has been fairly good, and they have each had a child. The son has already died young, and the daughter, named Peidi, is four years old. As the family grew, the expenses increased, and the expenditures became alarming. This year, when the Public Bus Company recruited female conductors, Xiuying was introduced and became conductor No. 76 in the company, earning a monthly salary to supplement the family income. There was a Cantonese man named Wu Dan, now twenty-three years old, who graduated from the Japanese Military Academy and now earns more than two hundred yuan a month. Wu recently came to Shanghai on business and always took the Shanghai South Public Bus. Therefore, he met Xiuying. Wu, seeing that Xiuying was attractive, made advances, and Xiuying, seeing that Wu was young and handsome, immediately favored him. Thus, the two fell in love. Recently, the heat between the two had reached the boiling point. However, the thought of her husband was an obstacle, and they could not do as they pleased. So, on September 7th of this year, she eloped behind her husband's back. After his wife disappeared, Li immediately hired people to search everywhere but could not find her. Until recently, someone secretly told him that Xiuying had privately met a man named Wu Dan and was now lodging with him in the Southeast Hotel next to the Great World. Li, upon hearing this news, was furious and immediately went to the hotel to inquire. The tea servant claimed that they had moved to Room No. 8 of the Datong Hotel at Wangjia Wharf in the South City. After hearing this, Li rushed to the destination at around 6 p.m. yesterday and called Gao Xigui, the guard on duty at Post 15, to enter with him. When he reached Room No. 8, he pushed the door open and saw Xiuying and Wu Dan lying on the same bed. He brought the man and woman back to the First Sub-Bureau of the First District. After a preliminary interrogation by the bureau chief, the case was deemed important, and he immediately ordered a written report to be submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau for investigation.

Violent Assault on Chengsongyang Long-Distance Bus

Men in Zhongshan Suits Act Unreasonably

Driver and Escorting Police Seriously Injured

All Drivers Guarantee Resumption of Work

At around 9:45 a.m. the day before yesterday, the No. 5 passenger bus of the Baoshan Chengsongyang Long-Distance Bus Company set off from Baoshan Station. When it was traveling on Nantongji Road, Sanguantang, Wusong, five or six men wearing Zhongshan suits flagged down the bus to pick them up to go to Songjiang. The bus driver, Zhou Ada, thought that the place was not a station, and he was afraid that stopping would delay the connection with the Songjiang-Shanghai train, so he ignored them and drove away quickly. When the bus arrived at Wusong Station to exchange passengers, and then set off from Songjiang Station, it drove back to Nantongji Road, Sanguantang, at around 10 a.m. Unexpectedly, the men were blocking the road, preventing the bus from moving forward. The driver had no choice but to stop the engine. The men immediately went forward to negotiate with the driver, Zhou Ada, saying why he did not stop the bus when they flagged it down but drove away quickly. Zhou then replied that this was not a station, and according to the company's regulations, he could not stop, and that the bus was full just now, so there was no way to accommodate them. He asked them to forgive him. Unexpectedly, the men became enraged and dragged Zhou out of the bus, punching and kicking him. At that time, Zhang Jiaxi, the police officer escorting the bus, saw the driver being beaten and went forward to persuade them, but he was also twisted and beaten severely. As a result, Zhou and Zhang's heads, faces, hands, feet, and other parts were seriously injured, and they fell to the road. The men then proceeded to smash the bus's engine parts and glass windows. There were more than ten male and female passengers in the bus, who were terrified at the sight and feared being affected, so they jumped out of the bus through the windows. After succeeding, the men leisurely fled south. After the incident, the long-distance bus company immediately sent a bus to the scene after receiving reports from passengers. The injured driver, Zhou Ada, and police officer Zhang Jiaxi, were sent to the hospital for treatment, and the damaged bus was towed back to the company for repair. At the same time, a report was filed with the County Public Security Bureau. After hearing the news, all the drivers of the bus company went on strike in protest of Zhou Ada being beaten and injured for no reason, demanding that the company request the authorities to investigate and deal with the murderers and provide guarantees for the future. If there was no satisfactory solution, they would not resume work. Although the company staff tried to persuade them, the drivers' attitude was very firm. As a result, from 10 a.m. the day before yesterday, all the scheduled passenger buses on the Songyang, Chengsong, and Chengyang lines were announced to be suspended for the whole day. Afterwards, Shen Jing, the Director of the Baoshan County Public Security Bureau, and Qian Tianpeng, the Director of the Construction Bureau, jointly went to the bus company to persuade the drivers, guaranteeing that the same incident would not happen again and promising to investigate and deal with the perpetrators. It was not until the night before last that all the drivers were satisfied and agreed to resume work the next day. Therefore, starting yesterday, the long-distance buses on the Chengsongyang lines have been operating as usual.

At 6:25 p.m. last night, four thugs arrived at No. 723 Miller Road, Hongkou. Three of them were carrying pistols and threatened the homeowner. When the housewife shouted for help, one of the robbers fired a shot, wounding the housewife. She bled profusely. The robbers, fearing the arrival of the police, fled in a hurry without stealing anything. The homeowner reported the incident to the police station in charge and requested an investigation.
